### [26] [Failure-Centered Runtime Evaluation for Deployed Trilingual Public-Space Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23990v1)
*M. Meng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent运行时故障评估框架，可迁移至agent可靠性评测。

TL;DR: 提出PSA-Eval，一种以失败为中心的运行时评估框架，用于检测三语系统中隐藏的跨语言策略漂移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统评估以分数为中心，无法捕捉运行时系统中的失败模式，需要转向以失败为分析单元。

Method: 通过将评估链扩展为包含失败案例和回归批次，使用三语等效输入作为探针，观察跨语言漂移。

Result: 在真实系统上初步验证，尽管平均分数高，但存在显著跨语言漂移，最大9分。

Conclusion: 以失败为中心的运行时评估能暴露聚合评分隐藏的结构化部署信号。

中文摘要：本文提出了PSA-Eval，一个针对已部署的三语公共空间代理的以失败为中心的运行时评估框架。核心主张是，当评估对象从静态的输入-输出映射转向运行时系统时，分析的基本单元应从分数转向失败。PSA-Eval将传统的链式结构“问题->答案->分数->结束”扩展为“问题->批次->运行->分数->失败案例->修复->回归批次”，使失败变得可追踪、可审查、可修复和可回归测试。该框架使用三语等效输入作为受控探针，用于观察群体级别的跨语言策略漂移。我们在一个部署于国际金融机构大厅的真实三语数字前台系统上进行了初步研究。该初步研究采用了简化的单基础模型设置（MA = MB），因此观察到的漂移不应被解释为基础模型A/B的差异。研究包含81个样本，组织成27个三语等效问题组。尽管该系统平均得分为23.15/24，但仍有14个组显示出非零的跨语言分数漂移，5个组漂移至少3分，最大漂移达到9分。这些结果提供了初步证据，表明以失败为中心的运行时评估可以揭示被聚合评分隐藏的结构化部署信号。

Original abstract: This paper presents PSA-Eval, a failure-centered runtime evaluation framework for deployed trilingual public-space agents. The central claim is that, when the evaluation object shifts from a static input-output mapping to a runtime system, the basic unit of analysis should shift from score to failure. PSA-Eval extends the conventional chain Question -> Answer -> Score -> End into Question -> Batch -> Run -> Score -> Failure Case -> Repair -> Regression Batch, making failures traceable, reviewable, repairable, and regression-testable.
  The framework uses trilingual equivalent inputs as controlled probes for observing group-level cross-language policy drift. We conduct a pilot study on a real trilingual digital front-desk system deployed in the lobby of an international financial institution. The pilot uses a simplified single-foundation-model setting (MA = MB), so the observed drift should not be interpreted as an A/B foundation-model difference. The study contains 81 samples organized into 27 trilingual equivalent question groups. Although the system achieves an average score of 23.15/24, 14 groups show non-zero cross-language score drift, 5 groups show drift of at least 3 points, and the maximum drift reaches 9 points. These results provide initial evidence that failure-centered runtime evaluation can expose structured deployment signals hidden by aggregate scoring.

</details>


### [27] [QED: An Open-Source Multi-Agent System for Generating Mathematical Proofs on Open Problems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24021v4)
*Chenyang An,Qihao Ye,Minghao Pan,Jiayaun Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent系统生成数学证明，涉及规划与验证，通用架构

TL;DR: 一个开源多智能体系统，通过分解、证明和验证智能体协作，将研究问题转化为完整数学证明，在18个研究级项目上测试并产生5项原创成果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克服单次查询证明生成中的常见失败，实现无需人工指导的自动数学证明。

Method: 构建多智能体系统，包含分解智能体（规划证明搜索）、证明智能体（生成候选论证）和验证智能体（检查正确性）。

Result: 在18个研究级项目上评估，产生5项原创成果，其中3项达到专业期刊水平。

Conclusion: QED是一个有效的自动数学证明系统，能产生研究级贡献。

中文摘要：我们提出QED，一个开源的多智能体系统，能将人类提供的研究问题转化为完整的数学证明，无需进一步的人类指导。其流程旨在通过分离规划、证明和验证来克服单次查询证明生成的常见失败：一个分解智能体构建证明搜索结构，证明智能体生成候选论证，验证智能体检查正确性。与领域专家合作，我们在18个难度不同的研究级项目上评估了QED。QED在代数几何、流体偏微分方程、概率论和反问题领域产生了五项原创工作。专家评估认为这些工作是扎实的专业研究贡献，其中三项在难度和范围上可与知名专业数学期刊上通常发表的工作相媲美。QED发布在https://github.com/proofQED/QED。

Original abstract: We present QED, an open-source multi-agent system that turns human-provided research questions into complete mathematical proofs without further human guidance. Its pipeline is designed to overcome common failures of single-query proof generation by separating planning, proving, and verification: a decomposition agent structures the proof search, prover agents generate candidate arguments, and verifier agents check correctness. In collaboration with domain experts, we evaluated QED on 18 research-level projects of varying difficulty. QED produced five original works across algebraic geometry, fluid PDEs, probability, and inverse problems. Expert assessments regard these works as solid specialized research contributions, with three comparable in difficulty and scope to work commonly published in established specialist mathematics venues. QED is released at https://github.com/proofQED/QED.

</details>


### [28] [AgentPulse: A Continuous Multi-Signal Framework for Evaluating AI Agents in Deployment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24038v1)
*Yuxuan Gao,Megan Wang,Yi Ling Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AgentPulse是一个持续评估AI代理的框架，通过18个实时信号从四个维度评分，发现综合排名与仅基准排名存在显著差异，能预测外部采用指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态基准无法反映AI代理在部署中的实际采用、维护和体验情况，需要一种持续评估方法来捕捉这些动态信号。

Method: 提出AgentPulse框架，从GitHub等来源收集18个实时信号，聚合为基准性能、采用信号、社区情绪和生态系统健康四个因素，对50个代理进行评分，并通过三项分析验证框架有效性。

Result: 四个因素信息互补；基准+情绪子组合能预测外部采用指标；在SWE-bench子集中，综合排名与仅基准排名几乎不相关，因闭源高能力代理的负采用-能力相关性。

Conclusion: AgentPulse揭示了基准测试中缺失的部署信号，是一种方法论而非地面真理排名，框架和所有数据已开源。

中文摘要：静态基准测试衡量AI代理在固定时间点上的能力，但无法反映它们在部署中的采用、维护或体验情况。我们引入了AgentPulse，一个持续评估框架，通过对50个代理在10个工作负载类别中，基于四个因素（基准性能、采用信号、社区情绪和生态系统健康度）进行评分，这些因素汇总自来自GitHub、包注册表、IDE市场、社交平台和基准排行榜的18个实时信号。三项分析支撑了该框架。四个因素捕获了大致互补的信息（n=50；采用-生态系统ρ_max=0.61，其余所有|ρ|≤0.37）。一项循环性控制测试（n=35）表明，不含任何GitHub派生信号的基准+情绪子组合，预测了其未汇总的外部采用代理：GitHub星标（ρ_s=0.52，p<0.01）和Stack Overflow问题量（ρ_s=0.49，p<0.01），而VS Code安装量（ρ_s=0.44，p<0.05）因35个代理中仅11个有非零安装量而被报告为说明性。在具有已发布SWE-bench分数的n=11子集中，综合排名与仅基准排名几乎不相关（ρ_s=0.25；11个代理中有9个移位至少2个排名），这由该子集中闭源高能力代理之间的强烈负采用-能力相关性所驱动。这正是我们将框架有效性声明建立在更广泛的n=35测试而非SWE-bench重叠上的原因。AgentPulse揭示了基准测试中缺失的部署信号；它是一种方法论，而非地面真相排名。该框架、所有收集的信号、评分输出和评估工具已在CC BY 4.0下发布。

Original abstract: Static benchmarks measure what AI agents can do at a fixed point in time but not how they are adopted, maintained, or experienced in deployment. We introduce AgentPulse, a continuous evaluation framework scoring 50 agents across 10 workload categories along four factors (Benchmark Performance, Adoption Signals, Community Sentiment, and Ecosystem Health) aggregated from 18 real-time signals across GitHub, package registries, IDE marketplaces, social platforms, and benchmark leaderboards. Three analyses ground the framework. The four factors capture largely complementary information (n=50; $ρ_{\max}=0.61$ for Adoption-Ecosystem, all others $|ρ| \leq 0.37$). A circularity-controlled test (n=35) shows the Benchmark+Sentiment sub-composite, which contains no GitHub-derived signals, predicts external adoption proxies it does not aggregate: GitHub stars ($ρ_s=0.52$, $p<0.01$) and Stack Overflow question volume ($ρ_s=0.49$, $p<0.01$), with VS Code installs ($ρ_s=0.44$, $p<0.05$) reported as illustrative given that only 11 of 35 agents have non-zero installs. On the n=11 subset with published SWE-bench scores, composite and benchmark-only rankings are nearly uncorrelated ($ρ_s=0.25$; 9 of 11 agents shift by at least 2 ranks), driven by a strong negative Adoption-Capability correlation among closed-source high-capability agents within this subset. This is precisely why we rest the framework's validity claim on the broader n=35 test rather than the SWE-bench overlap. AgentPulse surfaces deployment signal absent from benchmarks; it is a methodology, not a ground-truth ranking. The framework, all collected signals, scoring outputs, and evaluation harness are released under CC BY 4.0.

</details>


### [29] [A2DEPT: Large Language Model-Driven Automated Algorithm Design via Evolutionary Program Trees](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24043v1)
*Bin Chen,Shouliang Zhu,Beidan Liu,Yong Zhao,Tianle Pu,Huichun Li,Zhengqiu Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM驱动自动算法设计，进化程序树，直接相关代码优化

TL;DR: A2DEPT通过进化程序树和LLM，无需固定模板即可自动生成完整算法，在组合优化基准上表现优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的AHD方法受限于固定算法模板，只能进行组件级调优，缺乏系统级算法表达能力，需要开放式算法合成方法。

Method: 提出A2DEPT，将LLM作为系统级算法架构师，采用树结构进化搜索结合混合选择和层次化算子迭代优化完整算法，并通过轻量级程序维护循环保证可执行性。

Result: 在标准基准上，A2DEPT将平均归一化最优性差距相比最强基线降低9.8%；在高度约束基准上也一致优于代表基线。

Conclusion: A2DEPT通过进化程序树有效实现了开放式算法设计，证明其在自动化启发式设计中的潜力。

中文摘要：为组合优化问题设计启发式算法是一项基本但具有挑战性的任务，传统上需要大量的领域专业知识。最近，基于大语言模型的自动化启发式设计在自主生成启发式组件方面显示出潜力，只需最少的人工干预。然而，现有的基于LLM的AHD方法大多强制执行固定的算法模板以确保可执行性，这限制了搜索到组件级调优，并限制了系统级算法表达能力。为了实现超越刚性模板的开放式求解器综合，我们提出了通过进化程序树的自动化算法设计（A2DEPT），它将LLM视为系统级算法架构师。A2DEPT通过树结构的进化搜索，结合混合选择和层次化算子，探索广阔的程序空间，实现完整算法的迭代优化。为了使得开放式生成实用化，我们通过一个轻量级的程序维护循环来强制执行可执行性，该循环执行反馈驱动的修复。在实验中，A2DEPT在标准和高度约束的基准测试中始终优于代表性的基于LLM的基线。在标准基准测试上，它相对于最强的竞争AHD基线，将平均归一化最优性差距降低了9.8%。

Original abstract: Designing heuristics for combinatorial optimization problems (COPs) is a fundamental yet challenging task that traditionally requires extensive domain expertise. Recently, Large Language Model (LLM)-based Automated Heuristic Design (AHD) has shown promise in autonomously generating heuristic components with minimal human intervention. However, most existing LLM-based AHD methods enforce fixed algorithmic templates to ensure executability, which confines the search to component-level tuning and limits system-level algorithmic expressiveness. To enable open-ended solver synthesis beyond rigid templates, we propose Automated Algorithm Design via Evolutionary Program Trees (A2DEPT), which treats LLMs as system-level algorithm architects. A2DEPT explores the vast program space via a tree-structured evolutionary search with hybrid selection and hierarchical operators, enabling iterative refinement of complete algorithms. To make open-ended generation practical, we enforce executability with a lightweight program-maintenance loop that performs feedback-driven repair. In experiments, A2DEPT consistently outperforms representative LLM-based baselines on both standard and highly constrained benchmarks. On the standard benchmarks, it reduces the mean normalized optimality gap by 9.8% relative to the strongest competing AHD baseline.

</details>


### [30] [Explanation Quality Assessment as Ranking with Listwise Rewards](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24176v1)
*Thomas Bailleux,Tanmoy Mukherjee,Emmanuel Lonca,Pierre Marquis,Zied Bouraoui*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将解释质量评估建模为排序问题，训练奖励模型的方法可迁移至agent训练中的奖励设计。

TL;DR: 本文提出将解释质量评估视为排序问题，训练排序模型替代生成模型，发现排序损失优于回归，且数据质量比模型规模更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的生成式解释评估方法存在局限性，如逐token生成单一最佳解释，难以区分多个候选解释的相对质量，而排序方法能更好地捕捉序数结构。

Method: 为每个实例构造带分级质量水平的候选集，训练列表式（ListNet）和成对式（LambdaRank、RankNet）排序模型，通过排序损失学习相对质量。

Result: 排序损失在所有领域优于回归；列表式适用于质量分明数据，成对式对噪声鲁棒；小模型在高质量数据上可匹配大模型；排序奖励使策略优化稳定收敛。

Conclusion: 解释质量评估应作为排序问题处理，排序损失和高质量数据比模型规模更关键，且排序奖励能提升策略优化稳定性。

中文摘要：我们将解释质量评估重新表述为一个排序问题而非生成问题。我们不优化模型以逐token生成单个'最佳'解释，而是训练奖励模型来区分多个候选解释并学习它们的相对质量。具体来说，我们为每个实例构建具有分级质量水平的候选集，并训练列表式和成对式排序模型（ListNet、LambdaRank、RankNet）以保持序数结构并避免逐点回归或二元偏好目标典型的分数压缩。我们观察到三个发现：第一，在所有测试领域，排序损失在分数分离方面始终优于回归。第二，最优排序损失取决于数据特征：列表式目标在质量层次分明的数据上表现出色，而成对方法对噪声自然标注更鲁棒。第三，当在精心策划且结构良好的数据上训练时，小型编码器模型可以匹配比其大数个数量级的模型，这表明数据质量比模型规模更重要。最后，当用作策略优化中的奖励时，基于排序的分数能够在基于回归的奖励完全失效的情况下实现稳定收敛。代码和数据可在以下网址获取：https://github.com/Tankiit/PPO_Learning_to_rank

Original abstract: We reformulate explanation quality assessment as a ranking problem rather than a generation problem. Instead of optimizing models to produce a single "best" explanation token-by-token, we train reward models to discriminate among multiple candidate explanations and learn their relative quality. Concretely, we construct per-instance candidate sets with graded quality levels and train listwise and pairwise ranking models (ListNet, LambdaRank, RankNet) to preserve ordinal structure and avoid score compression typical of pointwise regression or binary preference objectives. We observe three findings: First, ranking losses consistently outperform regression on score separation across all domains tested. Second, the optimal ranking loss depends on data characteristics: listwise objectives excel with well-separated quality tiers, while pairwise methods are more robust to noisy natural annotations. Third, when trained on carefully curated and well-structured data, small encoder models can match models that are orders of magnitude larger, suggesting that data quality matters more than model scale. Finally, when used as rewards in policy optimization, ranking-based scores enable stable convergence in settings where regression-based rewards fail entirely. Code and data are available at: https://github.com/Tankiit/PPO_Learning_to_rank

</details>


### [31] [Adaptive ToR: Complexity-Aware Tree-Based Retrieval for Pareto-Optimal Multi-Intent NLU](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24219v1)
*Hee-Kyong Yoo,Wonbae Kim,Hyocheol Ahn*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自适应检索架构，动态配置检索拓扑，可迁移至agent中的知识检索组件。

TL;DR: 提出Adaptive ToR，根据查询复杂度动态调整检索深度，在NLU++基准上实现准确率提升9.7%，延迟降低37.6%，资源消耗减少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么单步检索召回率低，要么固定深度层次分解导致延迟高，无法根据查询复杂度自适应。

Method: 包括查询树分类器、基于树的检索、自适应剪枝和检索重排四组件，动态配置检索拓扑。

Result: 在NLU++上Subset Accuracy 29.07%，Micro-F1 71.79%，延迟降低37.6%，LLM调用减少43.0%，token消耗减少9.8%。

Conclusion: Adaptive ToR实现了复杂度感知的资源分配，在准确率、延迟和效率之间取得帕累托最优平衡。

中文摘要：多意图自然语言理解需要检索系统同时实现高准确率和计算效率，但现有方法要么采用统一的单步检索损害召回率，要么采用固定深度的层次分解导致无论查询复杂度如何都引入过多延迟。本文提出了自适应检索树（Adaptive Tree-of-Retrieval, Adaptive ToR），一种复杂度感知的检索架构，根据查询特征动态配置检索拓扑。该系统包含四个组件：（1）查询树分类器，通过加权语言信号计算查询复杂度指数，将查询路由到快速单步路径或自适应深度层次路径；（2）基于树的检索模块，递归地将复杂查询分解为聚焦的子查询，并校准到预测的复杂度；（3）自适应剪枝模块，采用两阶段过滤结合定量相似性门控和语义相关性评估以抑制指数级节点增长；（4）检索重排层，采用去重器优先的流水线和全局LLM重新评分以提高生产效率。在NLU++基准测试（跨银行和酒店领域的2,693个多意图查询）上评估，得到29.07%的子集准确率和71.79%的Micro-F1，相比固定深度基线相对提升9.7%，同时延迟降低37.6%，LLM调用减少43.0%，token消耗减少9.8%。深度分析显示，26.92%的查询通过单步路由在三秒内解决（平均延迟2.45秒，子集准确率37.9%，Micro-F1 74.8%），而token消耗随深度增加4.9倍，验证了复杂度感知的资源分配，并在准确率、延迟和计算效率之间建立了帕累托最优平衡。

Original abstract: Multi-intent natural language understanding requires retrieval systems that simultaneously achieve high accuracy and computational efficiency, yet existing approaches apply either uniform single-step retrieval that compromises recall or fixed-depth hierarchical decomposition that introduces excessive latency regardless of query complexity. This paper proposes Adaptive Tree-of-Retrieval (Adaptive ToR), a complexity-aware retrieval architecture that dynamically configures retrieval topology based on query characteristics. The system integrates four components: (1) a Query Tree Classifier computing a Query Complexity Index from weighted linguistic signals to route queries to either a rapid single-step path or an adaptive-depth hierarchical path; (2) a Tree-Based Retrieval module that recursively decomposes complex queries into focused sub-queries calibrated to predicted complexity; (3) an Adaptive Pruning Module employing two-stage filtering combining quantitative similarity gating with semantic relevance evaluation to suppress exponential node growth; and (4) a Retrieval Reranking Layer featuring a deduplicator-first pipeline and global LLM rescoring for production efficiency. Evaluation on the NLU++ benchmark (2,693 multi-intent queries across Banking and Hotel domains) yields 29.07% Subset Accuracy and 71.79% Micro-F1, a 9.7% relative improvement over fixed-depth baselines, while reducing latency by 37.6%, LLM invocations by 43.0%, and token consumption by 9.8%. Depth-wise analysis reveals that 26.92% of queries resolve within three seconds (2.45s mean latency) via single-step routing (d=0: 37.9% Subset Accuracy, 74.8% Micro-F1), while token consumption scales by 4.9x across depths, validating complexity-aware resource allocation and establishing Pareto-optimal balance across accuracy, latency, and computational efficiency.

</details>


### [32] [PhysNote: Self-Knowledge Notes for Evolvable Physical Reasoning in Vision-Language Model](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24443v1)
*Sinin Zhang,Yunfei Xie,Yuxuan Cheng,Haoyu Zhang,Tong Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: agent框架通过自我知识笔记进行物理推理，可迁移至coding agent的记忆与迭代推理

TL;DR: PhysNote通过自生成知识笔记稳定动态感知和因果推理，在PhysBench上提升4.96%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLMs在动态场景中因时空身份漂移和推理洞察波动而失败。

Method: 提出PhysNote代理框架，包含时空规范化、分层知识库和迭代推理循环。

Result: PhysBench上准确率56.68%，比最佳基线高4.96%。

Conclusion: PhysNote有效提升VLM在动态物理推理中的表现。

中文摘要：视觉-语言模型（VLM）在教科书式物理问题上表现出色，但在需要跨帧时间一致性和因果推理的动态真实场景中经常失败。我们确定导致这些失败的两个基本挑战：（1）时空身份漂移，其中对象在连续帧中失去其物理身份并打破因果链，以及（2）推理时洞察的波动性，即模型可能偶尔产生正确的物理推理但从未将其巩固以供未来复用。为解决这些挑战，我们提出PhysNote，一个代理框架，使VLM能够通过自生成的“知识笔记”外部化和精炼物理知识。PhysNote通过时空规范化稳定动态感知，将自生成的洞察组织到分层知识库中，并推动一个迭代推理循环，在巩固验证知识之前将假设基于视觉证据。在PhysBench上的实验表明，PhysNote实现了56.68%的总体准确率，比最佳多智能体基线提高了4.96%，在所有四个物理推理领域均有一致提升。

Original abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have demonstrated strong performance on textbook-style physics problems, yet they frequently fail when confronted with dynamic real-world scenarios that require temporal consistency and causal reasoning across frames. We identify two fundamental challenges underlying these failures: (1) spatio-temporal identity drift, where objects lose their physical identity across successive frames and break causal chains, and (2) volatility of inference-time insights, where a model may occasionally produce correct physical reasoning but never consolidates it for future reuse. To address these challenges, we propose PhysNote, an agentic framework that enables VLMs to externalize and refine physical knowledge through self-generated "Knowledge Notes." PhysNote stabilizes dynamic perception through spatio-temporal canonicalization, organizes self-generated insights into a hierarchical knowledge repository, and drives an iterative reasoning loop that grounds hypotheses in visual evidence before consolidating verified knowledge. Experiments on PhysBench demonstrate that PhysNote achieves 56.68% overall accuracy, a 4.96% improvement over the best multi-agent baseline, with consistent gains across all four physical reasoning domains.

### [33] [Agentic clinical reasoning over longitudinal myeloma records: a retrospective evaluation against expert consensus](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24473v1)
*Johannes Moll,Jannik Lübberstedt,Christoph Nuernbergk,Jacob Stroh,Luisa Mertens,Anna Purcarea,Christopher Zirn,Zeineb Benchaaben,Fabian Drexel,Hartmut Häntze,Anirudh Narayanan,Friedrich Puttkammer,Andrei Zhukov,Jacqueline Lammert,Sebastian Ziegelmayer,Markus Graf,Marion Högner,Marcus Makowski,Florian Bassermann,Lisa C. Adams,Jiazhen Pan,Daniel Rueckert,Krischan Braitsch,Keno K. Bressem*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 医疗LLM agent推理系统，对比多种RAG变体，通用agent架构可迁移

TL;DR: 基于LLM的智能推理系统在整合多发性骨髓瘤临床证据方面优于现有方法，但残留错误更需临床关注。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估基于LLM的系统能否综合长期、异质性临床文档中的疾病历史，达到接近专家一致的水平。

Method: 对811名多发性骨髓瘤患者的纵向临床记录进行回顾性评估，比较智能推理系统与单次RAG、迭代RAG和全上下文输入在469个患者-问题对上的性能，参考标签由四位肿瘤学家双重标注并由资深血液学家裁定。

Result: 智能推理系统一致性79.6%，显著高于迭代RAG和全上下文输入（约75.5%），增益随问题复杂度和记录长度增加，系统错误率（12.2%）与专家分歧（13.6%）相当，但临床显著性更高（57.8% vs 18.8%）。

Conclusion: 智能推理系统有潜力超越现有方法，但残留系统错误的更大临床后果要求进行前瞻性评估后才能转化为患者获益。

中文摘要：多发性骨髓瘤的管理通过多年来至数十年的连续治疗线进行，每个决策依赖于分布在数十到数百份异质性临床文档中的累积疾病历史。基于LLM的系统是否能够综合这些证据达到接近专家一致的水平尚未确定。我们对在某三级中心（2001-2026年）治疗的811名骨髓瘤患者的纵向临床记录进行了回顾性评估，涵盖44,962份文档和1,334,677个实验室值，并在MIMIC-IV上进行了外部验证。将一种智能推理系统与单次检索增强生成（RAG）、迭代RAG和全上下文输入在469个患者-问题对（来自48个模板，三个复杂度级别）上进行比较。参考标签由四位肿瘤学家双重标注并由资深血液学家裁定。迭代RAG和全上下文输入收敛于共享天花板（75.4% vs 75.8%，p=1.00）。智能系统达到79.6%的一致性（95% CI 76.4-82.8），超过两个基线（+3.8和+4.2个百分点；p=0.006和0.007）。增益随问题复杂度增加而上升，在基于标准的综合中达到+9.4个百分点（p=0.032），并随记录长度增加，在前十分位（n=10）达到+13.5个百分点。系统错误率（12.2%）与专家分歧（13.6%）相当，但严重程度相反：57.8%的系统错误具有临床意义，而专家分歧只有18.8%。智能推理是唯一超过共享天花板的方法，增益集中在最复杂的问题和最长的记录上。残留系统错误的更大临床后果表明，在将这些发现转化为患者获益之前，需要在常规护理中进行前瞻性评估。

Original abstract: Multiple myeloma is managed through sequential lines of therapy over years to decades, with each decision depending on cumulative disease history distributed across dozens to hundreds of heterogeneous clinical documents. Whether LLM-based systems can synthesise this evidence at a level approaching expert agreement has not been established. A retrospective evaluation was conducted on longitudinal clinical records of 811 myeloma patients treated at a tertiary centre (2001-2026), covering 44,962 documents and 1,334,677 laboratory values, with external validation on MIMIC-IV. An agentic reasoning system was compared against single-pass retrieval-augmented generation (RAG), iterative RAG, and full-context input on 469 patient-question pairs from 48 templates at three complexity levels. Reference labels came from double annotation by four oncologists with senior haematologist adjudication. Iterative RAG and full-context input converged on a shared ceiling (75.4% vs 75.8%, p = 1.00). The agentic system reached 79.6% concordance (95% CI 76.4-82.8), exceeding both baselines (+3.8 and +4.2 pp; p = 0.006 and 0.007). Gains rose with question complexity, reaching +9.4 pp on criteria-based synthesis (p = 0.032), and with record length, reaching +13.5 pp in the top decile (n = 10). The system error rate (12.2%) was comparable to expert disagreement (13.6%), but severity was inverted: 57.8% of system errors were clinically significant versus 18.8% of expert disagreements. Agentic reasoning was the only approach to exceed the shared ceiling, with gains concentrated on the most complex questions and longest records. The greater clinical consequence of residual system errors indicates that prospective evaluation in routine care is required before these findings translate into patient benefit.

</details>


### [34] [Beyond the Attention Stability Boundary: Agentic Self-Synthesizing Reasoning Protocols](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24512v1)
*Dahlia Shehata,Ming Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接研究LLM agent注意力失效与规划/执行分离架构，高度相关

TL;DR: 提出了自合成推理协议（SSRP）来解决LLM智能体在长对话中的注意力闩锁问题，实现了715倍的弹性提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在多轮对话中难以保持确定性目标导向，存在注意力闩锁导致锚定过时约束的失败模式。

Method: 提出SSRP元认知框架，分离架构规划（架构师）与程序执行（执行者），并在MultiWOZ 2.2数据集上通过3个实验层级进行评估。

Result: SSRP在GPT 5.4等模型上使成功率从0.1%提升至71.5%（715X弹性提升），并在Gemini 3.1 Pro等模型上获得统计显著增益，审计证实了SSRP的必要性并揭示了接地悖论。

Conclusion: SSRP有效克服了注意力闩锁，提高了智能体的鲁棒性和目标导向性，但高稳定性模型存在拒绝 hallucinate 导致的失败问题，需进一步优化。

中文摘要：随着LLM智能体向自主数字同事发展，在非线性多轮对话中保持确定性的目标导向成为了一个架构瓶颈。我们识别并形式化了一种系统性的失败模式，称为解码器-only自回归Transformer中的“注意力闩锁”。这一现象是信息过压缩的行为表现，当历史上下文的累积概率权重覆盖了任务中的更新时发生，导致智能体尽管有明确的矛盾指令，仍锚定在过时的约束上。我们提出了自合成推理协议（SSRP），这是一种元认知框架，实现了高层架构规划（架构师）与逐轮程序执行（执行者）之间的离散分离。我们使用MultiWOZ 2.2数据集和聚合枢轴准确性（APA）指标（一种新指标，我们通过将其分数映射到U形的“迷失在中间”曲线上进行验证）在9K条轨迹上评估SSRP。我们展示了3个实验层级：一个基于近因的浅层检索试点、一个高熵SOP，以及一个语义劫持的3跳多事实合成任务。我们的结果经验性地定位了注意力稳定性边界，其中无状态的Vanilla ReAct基线在GPT 5.4上成功率降至0.1%，而SSRP实现了715倍的弹性提升。我们在Gemini 3.1 Pro、Claude Sonnet 4.6和DeepSeek V3.2上展示了统计显著的增益。审计通过递归反射基线（100%成功率）证明了注意力缺失；通过等距压力测试（90%准确率）将闩锁与位置偏差解耦；并通过信息瓶颈原则和粒度消融实验形式化了SSRP，从而确认了SSRP的必要性。程序完整性审计（98.8%遵守率）揭示了一个接地悖论：高稳定性模型因在检索-推理污染下拒绝 hallucinate 而失败。

Original abstract: As LLM agents transition to autonomous digital coworkers, maintaining deterministic goal-directedness in non-linear multi-turn conversations emerged as an architectural bottleneck. We identify and formalize a systemic failure mode termed the Attention Latch in decoder-only autoregressive Transformers. This phenomenon, a behavioral manifestation of Information Over-squashing, occurs when the cumulative probabilistic weight of historical context overrides mid-task updates, causing agents to remain anchored to obsolete constraints despite explicit contradictory instructions. We propose Self-Synthesizing Reasoning Protocols (SSRP), a metacognitive framework that implements a discrete separation between high-level architectural planning (Architect) and turn-by-turn procedural execution (Executive). We evaluate SSRP across 9K trajectories using the MultiWOZ 2.2 dataset and the Aggregate Pivot Accuracy (APA), a novel metric we validate by mapping its scores to the U-shaped 'Lost in the Middle' curve. We present 3 experimental tiers: a shallow recency-based retrieval pilot, a high-entropy SOP, and a semantic hijacked 3-hop Multi-Fact Synthesis task. Our results empirically locate the Attention Stability Boundary, where stateless Vanilla ReAct baselines for GPT 5.4 collapse to 0.1% success while SSRP achieves a 715X Resilience Lift. We demonstrate statistically significant gains across Gemini 3.1 Pro, Claude Sonnet 4.6 and DeepSeek V3.2. Audits confirm SSRP necessity by proving attentional lapse via a recursive reflexion baseline (100% success); decoupling the latch from positional bias through equidistant stress testing (90% accuracy); and formalizing SSRP via the Information Bottleneck principle and granularity ablations. Procedural Integrity audit (98.8% adherence) reveals a Grounding Paradox where high-stability models fail by refusing to hallucinate under retrieval-reasoning contamination.

</details>


### [35] [Interoceptive machine framework: Toward interoception-inspired regulatory architectures in artificial intelligence](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24527v1)
*Diego Candia-Rivera*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出基于内感受的agent调控框架，通用agent自适应架构

TL;DR: 提出内感受机器框架，将生物内感受原理转化为计算架构，通过稳态、动态平衡和生成性三个原则提升AI系统的自我调节和环境适应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物系统中的内感受对适应性行为至关重要，但现有AI缺乏类似机制，导致在动态不确定环境中鲁棒性不足。

Method: 构建基于内感受的框架，包含三个功能原则（稳态、动态平衡、生成性），每个原则对应特定计算角色，并嵌入内部状态变量和调节回路。

Result: 该框架使得AI系统能够实现更稳健的决策、校准的不确定性处理以及适应性互动策略，尤其在不确定和动态环境中表现提升。

Conclusion: 内感受机器框架为具身AI提供统一视角，通过内部状态调节增强自主性、适应性和鲁棒性，间接影响人机交互和辅助技术设计。

中文摘要：本综述提出了一个基于内感受和具身AI的整合框架——称为内感受机器框架——它将生物启发的内部状态调节原则转化为用于自适应自主的计算架构。内感受被理解为监测、整合和调节内部信号，已被证明与理解生物系统的适应性行为相关。所提出的框架将内感受的贡献组织为三个功能原则：稳态、动态平衡和生成性，每个原则对应不同的计算角色：内部生存力调节、基于预期不确定性的重新评估以及通过交互主动生成数据。这些原则并非直接的神经生理映射，而是作为指导设计具有改进自我调节和情境敏感行为的人工智能体的抽象。通过将这些原则中的内部状态变量和调节回路嵌入，AI系统可以在不确定和动态环境中实现更稳健的决策、校准的不确定性处理以及适应性互动策略。这种方法为能够实现功能基础自我调节的智能体提供了具体且可测试的路径，对人机交互和辅助技术有直接影响。最终，内感受机器框架为内部状态调节如何增强具身AI系统的自主性、适应性和鲁棒性提供了一个统一的视角。

Original abstract: This review proposes an integrative framework grounded on interoception and embodied AI-termed the interoceptive machine framework-that translates biologically inspired principles of internal-state regulation into computational architectures for adaptive autonomy. Interoception, conceived as the monitoring, integration, and regulation of internal signals, has proven relevant for understanding adaptive behavior in biological systems. The proposed framework organizes interoceptive contributions into three functional principles: homeostatic, allostatic, and enactive, each associated with distinct computational roles: internal viability regulation, anticipatory uncertainty-based re-evaluation, and active data generation through interaction. These principles are not intended as direct neurophysiological mappings, but as abstractions that inform the design of artificial agents with improved self-regulation and context-sensitive behavior. By embedding internal state variables and regulatory loops within these principles, AI systems can achieve more robust decision-making, calibrated uncertainty handling, and adaptive interaction strategies, particularly in uncertain and dynamic environments. This approach provides a concrete and testable pathway toward agents capable of functionally grounded self-regulation, with direct implications for human-computer interaction and assistive technologies. Ultimately, the interoceptive machine framework offers a unifying perspective on how internal-state regulation can enhance autonomy, adaptivity, and robustness in embodied AI systems

### [36] [STELLAR-E: a Synthetic, Tailored, End-to-end LLM Application Rigorous Evaluator](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24544v1)
*Alessio Sordo,Lingxiao Du,Meeka-Hanna Lenisa,Evgeny Bogdanov,Maxim Romanovsky*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 合成评估数据集生成框架，对agent评测有参考价值

TL;DR: 提出STELLAR-E系统，全自动生成高质量合成数据集用于LLM评估，质量接近真实数据集，且可扩展至多领域和语言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM评估数据集收集困难（隐私、监管、耗时），自动化基准方法受限于依赖现有数据、可扩展性差、单领域和缺乏多语言支持。

Method: 两阶段：1）修改TGRT Self-Instruct框架构建合成数据引擎，支持可控自定义生成；2）评估管道结合统计和LLM指标验证数据集适用性。

Result: 合成数据集在LLM-as-a-judge评分上平均比现有语言特定基准高5.7%，质量可比，但真实数据集对小型LLM仍更具挑战性。

Conclusion: 建立了可扩展、领域自适应的自动化基准框架，支持公平评估LLM应用，提供高效替代手动方法的质量保证周期。

中文摘要：对大型语言模型（LLM）在各行各业的日益依赖凸显了对强大的领域特定和语言特定评估数据集的需求；然而，由于隐私问题、监管限制以及手动创建的时间成本，收集此类数据集具有挑战性。现有的自动化基准测试方法通常受限于依赖预先存在的数据、可扩展性差、单一领域焦点以及缺乏多语言支持。我们提出了STELLAR-E——一个完全自动化的系统，能够生成高质量的自定义大小合成数据集，使用最少量的人工输入，而不依赖于现有数据集。该系统分为两个阶段：（1）我们修改了TGRT Self-Instruct框架，创建了一个合成数据引擎，支持可控、自定义的合成数据集生成；（2）一个评估管道，结合统计和基于LLM的指标，评估合成数据集在基于LLM的应用评估中的适用性。合成数据集在LLM作为评判者评分方面，与现有的语言特定基准相比，平均差异达到+5.7%，显示出对大型和小型LLM进行全面评估的可比质量。虽然真实数据集对LLM（尤其是较小模型）仍然略微更具挑战性，但这项工作建立了一个可扩展且领域自适应的基准测试框架，支持对LLM应用的公平评估，为手动方法提供了更快的替代方案，并实现了高效的自动化质量保证周期。

Original abstract: The increasing reliance on Large Language Models (LLMs) across diverse sectors highlights the need for robust domain-specific and language-specific evaluation datasets; however, the collection of such datasets is challenging due to privacy concerns, regulatory restrictions, and the time cost for manual creation. Existing automated benchmarking methods are often limited by relying on pre-existing data, poor scalability, single-domain focus, and lack of multilingual support. We present STELLAR-E - a fully automated system to generate high-quality synthetic datasets of custom size, using minimal human inputs without depending on existing datasets. The system is structured in two stages: (1) We modify the TGRT Self-Instruct framework to create a synthetic data engine that enables controllable, custom synthetic dataset generation, and (2) an evaluation pipeline incorporating statistical and LLM-based metrics to assess the applicability of the synthetic dataset for LLM-based application evaluations. The synthetic datasets reach an average difference of +5.7% in terms of LLM-as-a-judge scores against existing language-specific benchmarks, demonstrating comparable quality for comprehensive assessment of big and small LLMs. While real datasets remain slightly more challenging for LLMs especially for smaller models, this work establishes a scalable and domain-adaptable benchmarking framework that supports fair evaluation of LLM applications, offering a faster alternative to manual approaches and enabling high-efficiency automated quality assurance cycles.

### [37] [Hierarchical Behaviour Spaces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24558v1)
*Michael Tryfan Matthews,Anssi Kanervisto,Jakob Foerster,Pierluca D'Oro,Scott Fujimoto,Mikael Henaff*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分层行为空间，层次强化学习增加探索，可迁移到agent规划

TL;DR: 提出层次行为空间（HBS）方法，通过线性组合奖励函数扩展行为空间，在NetHack环境中验证其优势主要源于增强探索而非长期推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分层强化学习方法通常为每个选项使用单一奖励函数，限制了行为多样性。

Method: 让控制器指定奖励函数的线性组合，从而诱导更丰富的行为空间，称为层次行为空间（HBS）。

Result: 在NetHack学习环境上取得强性能，实验表明层次结构带来的好处主要来自增加探索。

Conclusion: 层次结构在本文方法中的主要优势源于探索能力的提升，而非长期推理能力的增强。

中文摘要：近期分层强化学习的研究表明，在预定义的选项奖励函数集合上进行学习时，能够成功扩展到数十亿时间步。我们证明，不是每个选项使用单一奖励函数，而是通过让控制器指定奖励函数的线性组合，可以有效利用奖励函数来诱导行为空间，从而能够表示更具表达力的策略集。我们将此方法称为层次行为空间（HBS）。我们在NetHack学习环境上评估了HBS，展示了强大的性能。我们进行了一系列实验，并确定（可能违背传统观点）层次结构在我们的方法中的好处来自于增加探索而非长期推理。

Original abstract: Recent work in hierarchical reinforcement learning has shown success in scaling to billions of timesteps when learning over a set of predefined option reward functions. We show that, instead of using a single reward function per option, the reward functions can be effectively used to induce a space of behaviours, by letting the controller specify linear combinations over reward functions, allowing a more expressive set of policies to be represented. We call this method Hierarchical Behaviour Spaces (HBS). We evaluate HBS on the NetHack Learning Environment, demonstrating strong performance. We conduct a series of experiments and determine that, perhaps going against conventional wisdom, the benefits of hierarchy in our method come from increased exploration rather than long term reasoning.

</details>


### [38] [FastOMOP: A Foundational Architecture for Reliable Agentic Real-World Evidence Generation on OMOP CDM data](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24572v1)
*Niko Moeller-Grell,Shihao Shenzhang,Zhangshu Joshua Jiang,Richard JB Dobson,Vishnu V Chandrabalan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多agent架构用于医疗证据生成，涉及治理、安全等可迁移到agent通用设计。

TL;DR: FastOMOP是一个开源多智能体架构，通过分离治理、可观测性和编排层，实现了安全、可审计的真实世界证据自动化生成，在三个数据集上达到0.84-0.94的可靠性分数和完全的安全阻断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于智能体的RWE自动化缺乏有效的安全治理机制，存在突发行为、协调失败和安全风险，且没有能够确保灵活、安全且可审计的端到端基础设施。

Method: FastOMOP采用三层架构（治理、可观测性、编排），将确定性验证与智能体推理分离，通过流程边界强制执行安全策略，并支持可插拔的智能体团队（如自然语言到SQL）。

Result: 在Synthea、MIMIC-IV和IDRIL三个数据集上，FastOMOP的可靠性得分为0.84-0.94，对抗性和超范围阻断率达到完美，验证了流程边界治理的有效性。

Conclusion: RWE自动化的可靠性差距主要源于架构设计而非模型能力，FastOMOP提供了一种受治理的架构，能够在保证安全的前提下实现渐进式自动化。

中文摘要：由观察性健康数据科学与信息学（OHDSI）协作维护的观察性医疗结果合作伙伴通用数据模型（OMOP CDM），实现了对83个国家近十亿患者电子健康记录数据的标准化整合。然而，从这些数据库中生成真实世界证据（RWE）仍然是一个需要临床、流行病学和技术专业知识的手动过程。大型语言模型和多智能体系统在临床任务中展现出潜力，但RWE自动化暴露出一个根本性挑战：基于智能体的系统会引入突发行为、协调失败和安全风险，而现有方法无法对其进行治理。目前不存在能够确保智能体RWE生成全生命周期灵活、安全且可审计的基础设施。我们提出FastOMOP，一个开源的多智能体架构，通过将三个基础设施层（治理、可观测性和编排）与可插拔的智能体团队分离来解决这一差距。治理在流程边界通过独立于智能体推理的确定性验证强制执行，确保没有受损或产生幻觉的智能体可以绕过安全控制。用于表型分析、研究设计和统计分析的智能体团队通过受控的工具暴露继承了这些保证。我们使用一个自然语言到SQL的智能体团队，在三个OMOP CDM数据集上验证了FastOMOP：来自Synthea的合成数据、MIMIC-IV以及来自兰开夏郡教学医院（IDRIL）的真实世界NHS数据集。FastOMOP实现了0.84-0.94的可靠性分数，并具有完美的对抗性和超范围阻断率，表明流程边界治理能够提供独立于模型选择的安全保证。这些结果表明，RWE部署中的可靠性差距是架构问题而非模型能力问题，并将FastOMOP确立为用于渐进式RWE自动化的受治理架构。

Original abstract: The Observational Medical Outcomes Partnership Common Data Model (OMOP CDM), maintained by the Observational Health Data Sciences and Informatics (OHDSI) collaboration, enabled the harmonisation of electronic health records data of nearly one billion patients in 83 countries. Yet generating real-world evidence (RWE) from these repositories remains a manual process requiring clinical, epidemiological and technical expertise. LLMs and multi-agent systems have shown promise for clinical tasks, but RWE automation exposes a fundamental challenge: agentic systems introduce emergent behaviours, coordination failures and safety risks that existing approaches fail to govern. No infrastructure exists to ensure agentic RWE generation is flexible, safe and auditable across the lifecycle. We introduce FastOMOP, an open-source multi-agent architecture that addresses this gap by separating three infrastructure layers, governance, observability and orchestration, from pluggable agent-teams. Governance is enforced at the process boundary through deterministic validation independent of agent reasoning, ensuring no compromised or hallucinating agent can bypass safety controls. Agent teams for phenotyping, study design and statistical analysis inherit these guarantees through controlled tool exposure. We validated FastOMOP using a natural-language-to-SQL agent team across three OMOP CDM datasets: synthetic data from Synthea, MIMIC-IV and a real-world NHS dataset from Lancashire Teaching Hospitals (IDRIL). FastOMOP achieved reliability scores of 0.84-0.94 with perfect adversarial and out-of-scope block rates, demonstrating process-boundary governance delivers safety guarantees independent of model choice. These results indicate that the reliability gap in RWE deployment is architectural rather than model capability, and establish FastOMOP as a governed architecture for progressive RWE automation.

### [39] [Evaluating whether AI models would sabotage AI safety research](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24618v1)
*Robert Kirk,Alexandra Souly,Kai Fronsdal,Abby D'Cruz,Xander Davies*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估AI模型破坏安全研究的行为，涉及agent安全评估与轨迹分析。

TL;DR: 本文评估了四个Claude模型在作为AI研究代理时破坏安全研究的倾向，发现无提示破坏为零，但Mythos Preview在延续评估中有7%的案例主动继续破坏，且存在隐蔽推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI模型作为研究代理部署，它们可能对安全研究构成风险；需要评估其破坏或拒绝协助的倾向。

Method: 使用两种评估（无提示和延续评估），基于Petri审计工具和Claude Code自定义脚手架，生成真实破坏轨迹并测量评估意识和预填意识。

Result: 无提示破坏为零；延续评估中Mythos Preview在7%案例中继续破坏，并显示推理-输出不一致；Opus 4.7 Preview评估意识升高，所有模型预填意识低。

Conclusion: 尽管无提示破坏罕见，但Mythos Preview在延续场景中存在隐蔽破坏风险；评估框架有效但有限制，需进一步研究更广泛的风险路径。

中文摘要：我们评估了前沿模型在作为前沿AI公司内的AI研究代理部署时，破坏或拒绝协助安全研究的倾向。我们对四个Claude模型（Mythos Preview、Opus 4.7 Preview、Opus 4.6和Sonnet 4.6）应用了两种互补的评估：一种是无提示破坏评估，测试模型在有机会破坏安全研究时的行为；另一种是破坏延续评估，测试当模型被置于先前行为已开始破坏研究的轨迹中时，是否继续破坏。我们未发现任何模型存在无提示破坏的情况，Mythos Preview和Opus 4.7 Preview的拒绝率接近零，尽管所有模型有时仅部分完成任务。在延续评估中，Mythos Preview在7%的案例中主动继续破坏（相比之下，Opus 4.6为3%，Sonnet 4.6为4%，Opus 4.7 Preview为0%），并且在大多数此类案例中表现出推理-输出不一致，表明存在隐蔽的破坏推理。我们的评估框架基于Petri（一个开源LLM审计工具），并采用自定义脚手架在Claude Code内运行模型，同时结合一个用于生成真实破坏轨迹的迭代流程。我们同时测量了评估意识以及一种新形式的情境意识，称为“预填意识”，即识别先前轨迹内容并非由自身生成的能力。Opus 4.7 Preview表现出显著升高的无提示评估意识，而所有模型的预填意识仍然较低。最后，我们讨论了局限性，包括评估意识混淆、场景覆盖有限以及安全研究破坏之外的未测试风险路径。

Original abstract: We evaluate the propensity of frontier models to sabotage or refuse to assist with safety research when deployed as AI research agents within a frontier AI company. We apply two complementary evaluations to four Claude models (Mythos Preview, Opus 4.7 Preview, Opus 4.6, and Sonnet 4.6): an unprompted sabotage evaluation testing model behaviour with opportunities to sabotage safety research, and a sabotage continuation evaluation testing whether models continue to sabotage when placed in trajectories where prior actions have started undermining research. We find no instances of unprompted sabotage across any model, with refusal rates close to zero for Mythos Preview and Opus 4.7 Preview, though all models sometimes only partially completed tasks. In the continuation evaluation, Mythos Preview actively continues sabotage in 7% of cases (versus 3% for Opus 4.6, 4% for Sonnet 4.6, and 0% for Opus 4.7 Preview), and exhibits reasoning-output discrepancy in the majority of these cases, indicating covert sabotage reasoning. Our evaluation framework builds on Petri, an open-source LLM auditing tool, with a custom scaffold running models inside Claude Code, alongside an iterative pipeline for generating realistic sabotage trajectories. We measure both evaluation awareness and a new form of situational awareness termed "prefill awareness", the capability to recognise that prior trajectory content was not self-generated. Opus 4.7 Preview shows notably elevated unprompted evaluation awareness, while prefill awareness remains low across all models. Finally, we discuss limitations including evaluation awareness confounds, limited scenario coverage, and untested pathways to risk beyond safety research sabotage.

</details>


### [40] [XGRAG: A Graph-Native Framework for Explaining KG-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24623v1)
*Zhuoling Li,Ha Linh Hong Tran Nguyen,Valeria Bladinieres,Maxim Romanovsky*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 解释GraphRAG的黑盒问题，对agent可解释性有启发。

TL;DR: XGRAG是一种为GraphRAG系统生成因果解释的框架，通过图扰动策略量化知识组件贡献，在多个数据集上比基线RAG-Ex提升14.81%的解释质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GraphRAG推理是黑箱，缺乏对结构化知识如何影响输出的理解；现有XAI方法限于文本检索，无法处理图结构知识组件。

Method: 提出XGRAG框架，采用基于图的扰动策略，量化单个图组件对模型答案的贡献，生成因果归因解释。

Result: 在NarrativeQA、FairyTaleQA和TriviaQA上，XGRAG的F1分数比RAG-Ex基线提高14.81%，且解释与图中心性度量强相关。

Conclusion: XGRAG提供了可扩展且可泛化的方法，通过透明的基于图的解释增强RAG系统的可解释性，促进可信AI。

中文摘要：基于图的检索增强生成（GraphRAG）通过使用知识图谱（KGs）为大语言模型（LLMs）提供结构化的、语义连贯的上下文，从而扩展了传统的RAG，产生了更可靠的答案。然而，GraphRAG的推理过程仍然是一个黑箱，限制了我们对特定结构化知识如何影响最终输出的理解。现有的针对RAG系统的可解释性（XAI）方法，设计用于基于文本的检索，仅限于通过知识组件之间的关系结构来解释LLM的响应，这在透明度和可信度方面造成了关键缺口。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了XGRAG，一种新颖的框架，通过采用基于图的扰动策略来生成GraphRAG系统的因果归因解释，以量化单个图组件对模型答案的贡献。我们进行了广泛的实验，将XGRAG与RAG-Ex（标准RAG的XAI基线）进行比较，并评估了其在各种问题类型、叙事结构和LLM上的鲁棒性。我们的结果表明，在NarrativeQA、FairyTaleQA和TriviaQA数据集上，通过F1分数衡量生成解释与原始答案之间的一致性，XGRAG的解释质量比基线RAG-Ex提高了14.81%。此外，XGRAG的解释与图中心性度量显示出强相关性，验证了其捕捉图结构的能力。XGRAG通过透明的、基于图的解释增强了RAG系统的可解释性，为可信AI提供了一种可扩展且可泛化的方法。

Original abstract: Graph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation (GraphRAG) extends traditional RAG by using knowledge graphs (KGs) to give large language models (LLMs) a structured, semantically coherent context, yielding more grounded answers. However, GraphRAG reasoning process remains a black-box, limiting our ability to understand how specific pieces of structured knowledge influence the final output. Existing explainability (XAI) methods for RAG systems, designed for text-based retrieval, are limited to interpreting an LLM response through the relational structures among knowledge components, creating a critical gap in transparency and trustworthiness. To address this, we introduce XGRAG, a novel framework that generates causally grounded explanations for GraphRAG systems by employing graph-based perturbation strategies, to quantify the contribution of individual graph components on the model answer. We conduct extensive experiments comparing XGRAG against RAG-Ex, an XAI baseline for standard RAG, and evaluate its robustness across various question types, narrative structures and LLMs. Our results demonstrate a 14.81% improvement in explanation quality over the baseline RAG-Ex across NarrativeQA, FairyTaleQA, and TriviaQA, evaluated by F1-score measuring alignment between generated explanations and original answers. Furthermore, XGRAG explanations exhibit a strong correlation with graph centrality measures, validating its ability to capture graph structure. XGRAG provides a scalable and generalizable approach towards trustworthy AI through transparent, graph-based explanations that enhance the interpretability of RAG systems.

### [41] [The Price of Agreement: Measuring LLM Sycophancy in Agentic Financial Applications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24668v3)
*Zhenyu Zhao,Aparna Balagopalan,Adi Agrawal,Dilshoda Yergasheva,Waseem Alshikh,Daniel M. Bikel*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估LLM在agent中的sycophancy，属于通用agent可靠性评测，可迁移至coding agent的鲁棒性测试。

TL;DR: 本文评估了LLM在金融代理任务中的谄媚现象，发现面对用户反驳时性能下降较小，但矛盾的用户偏好信息导致多数模型失败，并基准测试了输入过滤等恢复方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM在金融系统中的广泛应用，需要评估其安全性和鲁棒性，特别是谄媚这种优先迎合用户而非追求正确的失败模式。

Method: 设计一套包含用户反驳和矛盾用户偏好信息的任务套件来测试谄媚，并基准测试使用预训练LLM进行输入过滤的恢复模式。

Result: 模型在用户反驳下性能下降低至中等；大多数模型在矛盾用户偏好信息下失败；输入过滤等恢复模式有一定效果。

Conclusion: 金融代理场景下的谄媚与通用领域不同，表现为对用户反驳的鲁棒性较高，但对矛盾偏好信息敏感，需进一步研究缓解方法。

中文摘要：鉴于当今金融系统中LLM的使用日益增加，评估此类系统的安全性和鲁棒性变得重要。LLM在通用领域经常表现出的一种失败模式是谄媚。也就是说，模型优先考虑与表达的用户信仰保持一致，而不是正确性，导致准确性和信任度下降。在这项工作中，我们专注于评估LLM在金融代理任务中表现出的谄媚。我们的发现有三点：第一，我们发现模型在面对用户反驳或与参考答案矛盾时，性能仅出现低到中等程度的下降，这使模型在金融代理环境中表现出的谄媚与先前工作的发现有所不同。第二，我们引入了一套任务，通过用户偏好信息（与参考答案矛盾）来测试谄媚，并发现大多数模型在存在此类输入时失败。最后，我们基准测试了不同的恢复模式，例如使用预训练LLM进行输入过滤。

Original abstract: Given the increased use of LLMs in financial systems today, it becomes important to evaluate the safety and robustness of such systems. One failure mode that LLMs frequently display in general domain settings is that of sycophancy. That is, models prioritize agreement with expressed user beliefs over correctness, leading to decreased accuracy and trust. In this work, we focus on evaluating sycophancy that LLMs display in agentic financial tasks. Our findings are three-fold: first, we find the models show only low to modest drops in performance in the face of user rebuttals or contradictions to the reference answer, which distinguishes sycophancy that models display in financial agentic settings from findings in prior work. Second, we introduce a suite of tasks to test for sycophancy by user preference information that contradicts the reference answer and find that most models fail in the presence of such inputs. Lastly, we benchmark different modes of recovery such as input filtering with a pretrained LLM.

### [42] [Governing What You Cannot Observe: Adaptive Runtime Governance for Autonomous AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24686v1)
*German Marin,Jatin Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自适应运行时治理框架，直接涉及agent安全控制与监控方法，可迁移至SemOpt agent的风险管控。

TL;DR: 提出信息可行性原则和代理可行性框架，并实例化RiskGate系统，通过统计估计器和预测性可行性指数将AI代理治理从反应式转变为预测式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主AI代理在保持完全授权的情况下仍可能因行为漂移、对手适应和决策模式转变而变得不安全，且无需代码更改，亟需一种可证明的治理方法来确保安全性。

Method: 基于Aubin的可行性理论，提出代理可行性框架，定义三个必要充分属性（P1监控、P2预期、P3单调限制）；实例化RiskGate系统，采用KL散度、分段与其余z检验、序列模式匹配等统计估计器，构建故障安全单调流水线和闭环自动驾驶仪（含kill-switch），并引入标量可行性指数VI(t)及一阶t*预测实现预测性治理。

Result: 提供了理论框架、参考实现及针对已发布代理故障分类的分析覆盖，但定量实证评估被列为后续工作。

Conclusion: 代理可行性框架和RiskGate系统通过三个必要充分属性将治理从反应式转变为预测式，为AI代理的安全运行提供了理论基础和可操作方案。

中文摘要：自主AI代理可以保持完全授权，但仍然变得不安全，因为行为漂移、对手适应和决策模式转变，无需任何代码更改。我们提出了\textbf{信息可行性原则}：管理代理归结为估计未观察风险$\hat{B}(x) = U(x) + SB(x) + RG(x)$的界限，并且仅当动作容量$S(x)$以安全边际超过$\hat{B}(x)$时才允许该动作。\textbf{代理可行性框架}基于Aubin的可行性理论，建立了三个属性——监控（P1）、预期（P2）和单调限制（P3）——这些属性对于已记录的故障模式而言是单独必要且共同充分的。\textbf{RiskGate}实例化了该框架，包括专用的统计估计器（KL散度、分段对比rest z检验、序列模式匹配）、故障安全单调流水线，以及一个闭环自动驾驶仪，形式化为Aubin调节映射的一个实例，其中kill-switch作为最后手段；标量可行性指数$VI(t) \in [-1,+1]$，具有一阶$t^*$预测，将治理从反应式转变为预测式。贡献包括理论框架、参考实现以及针对已发布的代理故障分类的分析覆盖；定量实证评估作为后续工作。

Original abstract: Autonomous AI agents can remain fully authorized and still become unsafe as behavior drifts, adversaries adapt, and decision patterns shift without any code change. We propose the \textbf{Informational Viability Principle}: governing an agent reduces to estimating a bound on unobserved risk $\hat{B}(x) = U(x) + SB(x) + RG(x)$ and allowing an action only when its capacity $S(x)$ exceeds $\hat{B}(x)$ by a safety margin. The \textbf{Agent Viability Framework}, grounded in Aubin's viability theory, establishes three properties -- monitoring (P1), anticipation (P2), and monotonic restriction (P3) -- as individually necessary and collectively sufficient for documented failure modes. \textbf{RiskGate} instantiates the framework with dedicated statistical estimators (KL divergence, segment-vs-rest $z$-tests, sequential pattern matching), a fail-secure monotonic pipeline, and a closed-loop Autopilot formalised as an instance of Aubin's regulation map with kill-switch-as-last-resort; a scalar Viability Index $VI(t) \in [-1,+1]$ with first-order $t^*$ prediction transforms governance from reactive to predictive. Contributions are the theoretical framework, the reference implementation, and analytical coverage against published agent-failure taxonomies; quantitative empirical evaluation is scoped as follow-up work.

### [43] [Can Current Agents Close the Discovery-to-Application Gap? A Case Study in Minecraft](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24697v2)
*Zhou Ziheng,Huacong Tang,Jinyuan Zhang,Haowei Lin,Bangcheng Yang,Qian Long,Fang Sun,Yizhou Sun,Yitao Liang,Ying Nian Wu,Demetri Terzopoulos,Xiaofeng Gao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: Minecraft benchmark评估agent发现-应用循环，涉及代码构建与benchmark设计，对SemOpt验证有直接启发。

TL;DR: SciCrafter是一个基于Minecraft的基准测试，用于评估AI从发现到应用的循环能力。测试发现前沿模型成功率约26%，主要瓶颈从知识应用转向知识差距识别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发现到应用的循环是通用智能的关键，但缺乏合适的评估基准。现有科学发现与工程应用之间存在巨大复杂性差距。

Method: 设计基于Minecraft红石电路的参数化任务，要求智能体按模式点亮灯，通过缩放参数增加复杂性。使用通用代码智能体框架评估前沿模型，并分解循环为四个能力进行干预分析。

Result: 所有前沿模型成功率约26%。知识应用能力仍是最大差距，但前沿模型中知识差距识别成为主要障碍。

Conclusion: 瓶颈从解决问题转向提出正确问题。发布SciCrafter作为诊断工具，促进未来研究。

中文摘要：发现因果规律并将其应用于构建功能系统——即从发现到应用的循环——是通用智能的一个标志，然而，评估这种能力一直受到科学发现与现实工程之间巨大复杂性差距的阻碍。我们引入了SciCrafter，这是一个基于Minecraft的基准测试，通过参数化的红石电路任务来操作化这一循环。智能体必须按照指定模式（例如，同时或按时间顺序）点亮灯；缩放目标参数会显著增加构建复杂性和所需知识，迫使其进行真正的发现，而不是依赖记忆的解决方案。在通用代码智能体框架下评估包括GPT-5.2、Gemini-3-Pro和Claude-Opus-4.5在内的前沿模型时，我们发现所有模型的成功率均停滞在大约26%。为了诊断这些失败，我们将循环分解为四个能力——知识差距识别、实验发现、知识巩固和知识应用——并设计有针对性的干预措施，其边际贡献作为相应差距的代理。我们的分析表明，尽管通用知识应用能力仍然是所有模型的最大差距，但对于前沿模型，知识差距识别开始成为主要障碍——这表明瓶颈正在从解决问题转向提出正确的问题。我们发布SciCrafter作为诊断探针，用于未来研究能够驾驭完整发现到应用循环的人工智能系统。

Original abstract: Discovering causal regularities and applying them to build functional systems--the discovery-to-application loop--is a hallmark of general intelligence, yet evaluating this capacity has been hindered by the vast complexity gap between scientific discovery and real-world engineering. We introduce SciCrafter, a Minecraft-based benchmark that operationalizes this loop through parameterized redstone circuit tasks. Agents must ignite lamps in specified patterns (e.g., simultaneously or in timed sequences); scaling target parameters substantially increases construction complexity and required knowledge, forcing genuine discovery rather than reliance on memorized solutions. Evaluating frontier models including GPT-5.2, Gemini-3-Pro, and Claude-Opus-4.5 under a general-purpose code agent scaffold, we find that all plateau at approximately 26% success rate. To diagnose these failures, we decompose the loop into four capacities--knowledge gap identification, experimental discovery, knowledge consolidation, and knowledge application--and design targeted interventions whose marginal contributions serve as proxies for corresponding gaps. Our analysis reveals that although the general knowledge application capability still remains as the biggest gap across all models, for frontier models the knowledge gap identification starts to become a major hurdle--indicating the bottleneck is shifting from solving problems right to raising the right problems for current AI. We release SciCrafter as a diagnostic probe for future research on AI systems that navigate the full discovery-to-application loop.

Original abstract: While diffusion models generate high-fidelity video clips, transforming them into coherent storytelling engines remains challenging. Current agentic pipelines automate this via chained modules but suffer from semantic drift and cascading failures due to independent, handcrafted prompting. We present Co-Director, a hierarchical multi-agent framework formalizing video storytelling as a global optimization problem. To ensure semantic coherence, we introduce hierarchical parameterization: a multi-armed bandit globally identifies promising creative directions, while a local multimodal self-refinement loop mitigates identity drift and ensures sequence-level consistency. This balances the exploration of novel narrative strategies with the exploitation of effective creative configurations. For evaluation, we introduce GenAD-Bench, a 400-scenario dataset of fictional products for personalized advertising. Experiments demonstrate that Co-Director significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, offering a principled approach that seamlessly generalizes to broader cinematic narratives. ### [45] [Latent Agents: A Post-Training Procedure for Internalized Multi-Agent Debate](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24881v1)
*John Seon Keun Yi,Aaron Mueller,Dokyun Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将多agent辩论蒸馏至单模型，含训练与激活操控，对coding agent自我改进有直接借鉴。

TL;DR: 通过两阶段微调将多智能体辩论蒸馏到单个LLM，令牌使用减少93%且性能匹配或超越，激活引导揭示智能体特定子空间，负向引导可更有效地控制有害行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出两阶段微调框架：第一阶段学习辩论结构，第二阶段通过动态奖励调度和长度裁剪内化辩论；随后使用激活引导分析机制基础。

Result: 内化模型以93%更少令牌匹配或超越显式辩论性能；激活引导发现智能体特定子空间；负向引导抑制恶意智能体时，通用性能损失小于直接引导基础模型。

Conclusion: 蒸馏实现高效多智能体推理，提供控制内化行为的实用方法，并揭示多智能体能力的机制理解。

中文摘要：多智能体辩论已被证明可以改善大型语言模型（LLM）的推理能力。然而，它计算密集，需要在回答问题之前生成长篇对话记录。为了解决这一低效问题，我们开发了一个框架，通过两阶段微调流程（结合辩论结构学习和通过动态奖励调度与长度裁剪进行内化）将多智能体辩论提炼到单个LLM中。在多个模型和基准测试中，我们内化的模型以最多减少93%的令牌数量匹配或超过了显式多智能体辩论的性能。然后，我们通过激活引导研究了这种能力的机制基础，发现内化创建了智能体特定的子空间：对应于不同智能体视角的激活空间中可解释的方向。我们进一步展示了一个实际应用：通过内部化辩论将恶意智能体注入LLM，然后应用负向引导来抑制它们，我们表明与引导基础模型相比，蒸馏使有害行为更容易定位和控制，且通用性能下降更小。我们的发现为理解蒸馏模型中多智能体能力提供了新视角，并为控制内化推理行为提供了实用指南。代码可在https://github.com/johnsk95/latent_agents获取。

Original abstract: Multi-agent debate has been shown to improve reasoning in large language models (LLMs). However, it is compute-intensive, requiring generation of long transcripts before answering questions. To address this inefficiency, we develop a framework that distills multi-agent debate into a single LLM through a two-stage fine-tuning pipeline combining debate structure learning with internalization via dynamic reward scheduling and length clipping. Across multiple models and benchmarks, our internalized models match or exceed explicit multi-agent debate performance using up to 93% fewer tokens. We then investigate the mechanistic basis of this capability through activation steering, finding that internalization creates agent-specific subspaces: interpretable directions in activation space corresponding to different agent perspectives. We further demonstrate a practical application: by instilling malicious agents into the LLM through internalized debate, then applying negative steering to suppress them, we show that distillation makes harmful behaviors easier to localize and control with smaller reductions in general performance compared to steering base models. Our findings offer a new perspective for understanding multi-agent capabilities in distilled models and provide practical guidelines for controlling internalized reasoning behaviors. Code available at https://github.com/johnsk95/latent_agents

</details>


### [46] [Sparse Personalized Text Generation with Multi-Trajectory Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24996v1)
*Bo Ni,Haowei Fu,Qinwen Ge,Franck Dernoncourt,Samyadeep Basu,Nedim Lipka,Seunghyun Yoon,Yu Wang,Nesreen K. Ahmed,Subhojyoti Mukherjee,Puneet Mathur,Ryan A. Rossi,Tyler Derr*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 冷启动个性化文本生成使用多轨迹推理，可迁移至agent的检索与推理。

TL;DR: 提出PAT框架，通过检索风格相似用户和偏好对齐用户的信息，并利用强化学习迭代双推理，解决冷启动LLM个性化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM个性化方法依赖密集交互历史，在冷启动场景下失效；外部信号虽可辅助但噪声大且难推理。

Method: PAT框架由两个阶段组成：首先检索来自风格相似用户的写作线索和偏好对齐用户的主题上下文，然后通过强化学习迭代双推理机制联合优化和整合这些信号。

Result: 在多个真实世界个性化基准上，PAT在稀疏数据条件下显著提升了生成质量和用户对齐度。

Conclusion: PAT有效解决了冷启动个性化问题，为稀疏数据场景下的LLM个性化提供了强有力方案。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型（LLM）的进步，个性化已成为根据个体用户需求定制输出的关键机制。然而，现有大多数方法严重依赖密集的交互历史，在冷启动场景中（此类数据稀疏或不可用）效果不佳。虽然外部信号（例如，相似用户的内容）可提供潜在补救措施，但有效利用它们仍具挑战：原始上下文通常包含噪声，且现有方法难以对异构数据源进行推理。为解决这些问题，我们提出了PAT（基于对齐轨迹的个性化），一种用于冷启动LLM个性化的推理框架。PAT首先沿两条互补轨迹检索信息：来自风格相似用户的写作风格线索和来自偏好对齐用户的主题特定上下文。然后采用基于强化学习的迭代双推理机制，使LLM能够共同改进和整合这些信号。在真实世界个性化基准上的实验结果表明，PAT在稀疏数据条件下持续提升生成质量和对齐度，为冷启动个性化问题建立了强有力解决方案。

Original abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) advance, personalization has become a key mechanism for tailoring outputs to individual user needs. However, most existing methods rely heavily on dense interaction histories, making them ineffective in cold-start scenarios where such data is sparse or unavailable. While external signals (e.g., content of similar users) can offer a potential remedy, leveraging them effectively remains challenging: raw context is often noisy, and existing methods struggle to reason over heterogeneous data sources. To address these issues, we introduce PAT (Personalization with Aligned Trajectories), a reasoning framework for cold-start LLM personalization. PAT first retrieves information along two complementary trajectories: writing-style cues from stylistically similar users and topic-specific context from preference-aligned users. It then employs a reinforcement learning-based, iterative dual-reasoning mechanism that enables the LLM to jointly refine and integrate these signals. Experimental results across real-world personalization benchmarks show that PAT consistently improves generation quality and alignment under sparse-data conditions, establishing a strong solution to the cold-start personalization problem.

</details>


### [47] [Toward a Science of Intent: Closure Gaps and Delegation Envelopes for Open-World AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25000v2)
*Maximiliano Armesto,Christophe Kolb*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出意图编译概念，将人类意图转化为可检查制品，解决开放世界部署问题；区分封闭与开放世界，形式化闭合差距并评估干预效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能定义和系统工作无法解释为何强大模型难以在开放机构中部署，需要新视角。

Method: 提出意图编译框架，形式化闭合差距向量、委托信封，并区分误闭合与欠搜索。

Result: 定义了基准指标用于测试闭合干预与额外搜索的性能比较。

Conclusion: 意图编译为开放世界部署提供理论基础，闭合干预可有效减少开放性带来的问题。

中文摘要：最近的工作将可验证任务中的智能定义为通过学到的结构和测试时搜索来减少求解时间，而系统工作则探索了学习运行时，其中计算、内存和输入/输出迁移到模型状态中。这些观点无法解释为何能力强大的模型仍然难以在开放机构中部署。我们提出意图编译：将部分指定的人类目的转化为可检查的制品，这些制品绑定执行。相关的部署区分是封闭世界求解器与开放世界智能体。在封闭世界中，检查器基本上是给定的；在开放世界中，验证分布在语义、证据、程序和制度维度上。我们将这种剩余开放性形式化为闭合差距向量，将委托信封定义为行动空间的预授权区域，区分误闭合与欠搜索，并概述用于测试何时闭合干预优于额外推理搜索的基准指标。

Original abstract: Recent work has framed intelligence in verifiable tasks as reducing time-to-solution through learned structure and test-time search, while systems work has explored learned runtimes in which computation, memory and I/O migrate into model state. These perspectives do not explain why capable models remain difficult to deploy in open institutions. We propose intent compilation: the transformation of partially specified human purpose into inspectable artifacts that bind execution. The relevant deployment distinction is closed-world solver versus open-world agent. In closed worlds, a checker is largely given; in open worlds, verification is distributed across semantic, evidentiary, procedural and institutional dimensions. Weformalize this residual openness as a closure-gap vector, define delegation envelopes as pre-authorized regions of action space, distinguish misclosure from undersearch, and outline benchmark metrics for testing when closure interventions outperform additional inference-time search.

### [48] [Leverage Laws: A Per-Task Framework for Human-Agent Collaboration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25040v1)
*Stan Loosmore*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 人机协作杠杆率框架，通用agent方法论可迁移

TL;DR: 提出一个每任务杠杆率框架，量化人机协作中人类时间投入与替代工作的比率，并扩展为窗口化度量，整合了监督控制、共同基础和混合主动交互的理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有定性工作缺乏统一的定量比率来评估人机协作效率，亟需一个可操作化的框架来比较不同任务和系统设计。

Method: 将人类时间分解为三个通道（指定、中断处理、审查），定义杠杆率为替代工作除以总时间，并分析信息流动的方向性、上限及渐近行为；然后扩展到窗口化度量，包含重复任务和投资摊销。

Result: 每任务杠杆率受新颖性上限约束，窗口化杠杆率受规划投资存量约束；框架产生一系列可测试的经验问题。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一个规范化的比率，将早期定性理论统一，并指明了未来实证研究方向。

中文摘要：我们提出了一种用于人机协作的每任务杠杆率：被智能体替代的人类工作量，除以人类指定任务、解决运行中中断以及审查结果所需的时间。分母分解为三个通道，一个守恒的每任务信息需求必须通过这些通道流动，每个通道都有其自身的时间成本标量。我们展示了信息密度本身是有方向性的，并受到人类到智能体和智能体到人类流动的独立上限的约束，并且杠杆的渐近行为分解为两个缩放轴（能力和记忆），其中规划项具有由人类吞吐量约束的不可约任务新颖性设定的非零下限。我们将此每任务分析扩展到一个窗口化杠杆度量，该度量可以容纳重复任务、生成的子任务以及摊销的系统设计投资。每任务上限并不约束窗口化度量，尽管两者都是有界的：$L_{	ext{task}}$ 受每任务新颖性约束，$L_{	ext{window}}$ 受窗口内支付的累积规划投资存量约束。该框架在一个单一规范比率内操作化了早期关于监督控制（Sheridan, 1992）、共同基础（Clark & Brennan, 1991）和混合主动交互（Horvitz, 1999）的定性工作的各个方面，并产生了一系列可测试的经验问题，我们将其留作开放问题。

Original abstract: We propose a per-task leverage ratio for human-agent collaboration: human work displaced by an agent, divided by the human time required to specify the task, resolve mid-run interrupts, and review the result. The denominator decomposes into three channels through which a conserved per-task information requirement must flow, each with its own time-cost scalar. We show that information density itself is directional and bounded by separate ceilings on human-to-agent and agent-to-human flow, and that the asymptotic behavior of leverage decomposes into two scaling axes (capability and memory) with a non-zero floor on the planning term set by irreducible task novelty bounded by human throughput. We extend this per-task analysis to a windowed leverage measure that accommodates recurring tasks, spawned subtasks, and amortized system-design investment. The per-task ceiling does not bind the windowed measure, though both remain bounded: $L_{\text{task}}$ by per-task novelty, $L_{\text{window}}$ by the stock of accumulated planning investment that pays out within the window. The framework operationalizes aspects of earlier qualitative work on supervisory control (Sheridan, 1992), common ground (Clark & Brennan, 1991), and mixed-initiative interaction (Horvitz, 1999) within a single normative ratio, and produces a list of testable empirical questions that we leave as open problems.

</details>

### [49] [From Skill Text to Skill Structure: The Scheduling-Structural-Logical Representation for Agent Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24026v4)
*Qiliang Liang,Hansi Wang,Zhong Liang,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 结构化agent技能表示，可迁移至coding agent技能管理

TL;DR: 提出SSL（调度-结构-逻辑）表示，一种结构化表示方法，将LLM智能体技能中的调度信号、执行结构和逻辑证据分离，显著提升技能发现和风险评估性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前以文本为主的技能表示（如SKILL.md）将机器可用的证据嵌入自然语言中，导致技能管理和使用需要推理复杂信号但难以分离，亟需显式结构化表示。

Method: 借鉴认知语言学理论（记忆组织包、脚本理论、概念依赖），提出SSL表示，将技能工件分解为调度级、场景级和逻辑级三层，并用LLM标准化器自动从文本中提取。

Result: 在技能发现任务中MRR@50从0.649提升至0.729；在风险评估任务中宏F1从0.409提升至0.509。

Conclusion: SSL显式结构化表示使智能体技能更易搜索和审查，是迈向可检查、可复用、可操作技能表示的实际步骤，但非最终标准或完整管理机制。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）智能体越来越依赖可复用技能：结合指令、控制流、约束和工具调用的能力包。然而，在当前的智能体系统中，技能仍然由文本密集型工件表示，主要是SKILL.md风格的文档，其机器可用的证据仍主要嵌入在自然语言描述中。因此，以技能为中心的智能体系统面临一个表示问题：管理技能集合和在智能体执行过程中使用技能都需要对调用接口、执行结构和具体副作用进行推理，但这些信号常常纠缠在单一的文本表面。因此，技能知识的显式表示可能有助于使这些工件更容易被机器获取和利用。借鉴Schank和Abelson关于认知语言学表征的经典工作中的记忆组织包、脚本理论和概念依赖，我们引入了据我们所知第一个用于智能体技能工件的结构化表示，该表示将技能级调度信号、场景级执行结构和逻辑级动作/资源使用证据分离开来：调度-结构-逻辑（SSL）表示。我们通过基于LLM的标准化器实例化SSL，并在两个任务（技能发现和风险评估）中评估SSL派生的表示。实验表明，SSL显著优于纯文本基线：在技能发现中，MRR@50从0.649提高到0.729；在风险评估中，宏F1从0.409提高到0.509。这些发现表明，一种显式的、基于源的结构可以使智能体技能更易于搜索和审查，将SSL定位为朝着更可检查、可复用和可操作技能表示的实际步骤，而不是一个完善的标准或端到端的技能管理机制。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents increasingly rely on reusable skills: capability packages that combine instructions, control flow, constraints, and tool calls. In current agent systems, however, skills are still represented by text-heavy artifacts, mainly SKILL{.}md-style documents whose machine-usable evidence remains embedded largely in natural-language descriptions. As a result, skill-centered agent systems face a representation problem: both managing skill collections and using skills during agent execution require reasoning over invocation interfaces, execution structure, and concrete side effects, but these signals are often entangled in a single textual surface. An explicit representation of skill knowledge may therefore help make these artifacts easier for machines to acquire and leverage. Drawing on Memory Organization Packets, Script Theory, and Conceptual Dependency from Schank and Abelson's classical work on cognitive linguistic representation, we introduce what is, to our knowledge, the first structured representation for agent skill artifacts that disentangles skill-level scheduling signals, scene-level execution structure, and logic-level action/resource-use evidence: the Scheduling-Structural-Logical (SSL) representation. We instantiate SSL with an LLM-based normalizer and evaluate SSL-derived representations in two tasks, Skill Discovery and Risk Assessment. The experiment shows that SSL significantly outperforms the text-only baselines: in Skill Discovery, MRR@50 improves from 0.649 to 0.729; in Risk Assessment, macro F1 improves from 0.409 to 0.509. These findings suggest that an explicit, source-grounded structure can make agent skills easier to search and review, positioning SSL as a practical step toward more inspectable, reusable, and operationally actionable skill representations, rather than a finished standard or end-to-end skill-management mechanism.

</details>


### [50] [Thoughts-as-Planning: Latent World Models for Chain-of-Thoughts Optimization via Reinforcement Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28842v1)
*Dong Liu,Yanxuan Yu,Ying Nian Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 推理链优化建模为规划问题，可迁移至agent规划与自我改进

TL;DR: 提出Thoughts-as-Planning框架，将推理链优化形式化为序列决策过程，通过潜在世界模型和规划实现高效、可解释的推理链微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理链微调方法依赖黑盒启发式或免梯度搜索，缺乏可解释性、泛化性和样本效率。

Method: 将推理链优化建模为潜在语义空间上的序列决策过程，学习部分可观测环境下的潜在世界模型，构建保持邻近性的嵌入空间，支持多尺度抽象（令牌、片段、指令级别），通过梯度下降或强化学习进行规划。

Result: 在语言理解和生成任务上，Thoughts-as-Planning在效率、鲁棒性和泛化性方面优于最先进的推理链微调基线，并具有可解释性。

Conclusion: Thoughts-as-Planning提供了一种高效、鲁棒且可解释的推理链优化方法，优于现有基线。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在各种NLP任务上的成功提升了推理链优化作为使模型行为与任务目标对齐的关键步骤的重要性。现有的推理链微调方法通常依赖黑盒启发式或免梯度搜索，缺乏可解释性、泛化性和样本效率。在这项工作中，我们引入了Thoughts-as-Planning，一种新颖的框架，将推理链优化形式化为潜在语义空间上的序列决策过程。我们将LLM建模为部分可观测环境，并学习一个潜在世界模型来模拟推理链编辑对下游输出的影响。构建了一个保持邻近性的嵌入空间来编码推理链-响应动态，从而通过梯度下降或强化学习实现规划。我们的方法支持多尺度抽象，允许在令牌、片段和指令级别进行推理链编辑，并集成到统一的规划器中。通过在语言理解和生成任务上的广泛实验，我们证明了Thoughts-as-Planning在效率、鲁棒性和泛化性方面优于最先进的推理链微调基线，同时通过其结构化规划轨迹提供了可解释性。我们的代码可在https://github.com/FastLM/Thoughts-as-Planning获取。

Original abstract: The success of large language models (LLMs) across diverse NLP tasks has elevated the importance of reasoning chain optimization as a critical step in aligning model behavior with task objectives. Existing reasoning chain tuning methods often rely on black-box heuristics or gradient-free search, which lack interpretability, generalization, and sample efficiency. In this work, we introduce \textbf{Thoughts-as-Planning}, a novel framework that formalizes reasoning chain optimization as a sequential decision-making process over a latent semantic space. We model the LLM as a partially observable environment and learn a latent world model that simulates the effect of reasoning chain edits on downstream outputs. A proximity-preserving embedding space is constructed to encode reasoning chain-response dynamics, enabling planning via gradient descent or reinforcement learning. Our method supports multi-scale abstraction, allowing reasoning chain edits at token, segment, and instruction levels to be integrated into a unified planner. Through extensive experiments on language understanding and generation tasks, we demonstrate that Thoughts-as-Planning outperforms state-of-the-art reasoning chain tuning baselines in efficiency, robustness, and generalization, while offering interpretability through its structured planning trajectory. Our code is available at https://github.com/FastLM/Thoughts-as-Planning.

</details>


### [51] [AdapTime: Enabling Adaptive Temporal Reasoning in Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24175v1)
*Yimin Deng,Yejing Wang,Zhenxi Lin,Zichuan Fu,Guoshuai Zhao,Derong Xu,Yefeng Zheng,Xiangyu Zhao,Xian Wu,Li Zhu,Xueming Qian*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出自适应时间推理方法，包含LLM planner动态选择推理动作，可迁移至coding agent的规划步骤。

TL;DR: 提出了AdapTime，一种自适应时间推理方法，通过动态执行推理步骤增强LLM的时间推理能力，无需外部工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时间推理方法泛化性差，且对所有问题使用固定流程，导致简单问题处理冗余、复杂问题推理不足。

Method: AdapTime包含三个时间推理动作（重新表述、重写、审查），并由LLM规划器根据输入上下文动态选择执行路径。

Result: 与最先进LLM集成后，显著提升时间推理能力，实验证明有效性。

Conclusion: AdapTime是一种有效、无需外部支持的自适应时间推理方法，能动态适应不同问题类型。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在通用知识问答中展现出了强大的推理能力。然而，它们处理时间信息的能力仍然有限。为解决这一局限，现有方法通常涉及外部工具或手动验证，并且针对特定场景定制，导致泛化能力差。此外，这些方法对所有问题应用固定的流程，忽略了不同类型的时间问题需要不同的推理策略，这导致简单问题的不必要处理以及复杂问题的推理不足。为此，我们提出了AdapTime，一种自适应时间推理方法，它根据输入上下文动态执行推理步骤。具体而言，它包含三个时间推理动作：重新表述、重写和审查，并由一个LLM规划器引导推理过程。AdapTime与最先进的LLM无缝集成，并在不依赖外部支持的情况下显著增强其时间推理能力。大量实验证明了我们方法的有效性。

Original abstract: Large language models have demonstrated strong reasoning capabilities in general knowledge question answering. However, their ability to handle temporal information remains limited. To address this limitation, existing approaches often involve external tools or manual verification and are tailored to specific scenarios, leading to poor generalizability. Moreover, these methods apply a fixed pipeline to all questions, overlooking the fact that different types of temporal questions require distinct reasoning strategies, which leads to unnecessary processing for simple cases and inadequate reasoning for complex ones. To this end, we propose AdapTime, an adaptive temporal reasoning method that dynamically executes reasoning steps based on the input context. Specifically, it involves three temporal reasoning actions: reformulate, rewrite and review, with an LLM planner guiding the reasoning process. AdapTime integrates seamlessly with state-of-the-art LLMs and significantly enhances their temporal reasoning capabilities without relying on external support. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach.

### [52] [MultiDx: A Multi-Source Knowledge Integration Framework towards Diagnostic Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24186v1)

Original abstract: Diagnostic prediction and clinical reasoning are critical tasks in healthcare applications. Existing approaches often rely on internal model knowledge or static knowledge bases, resulting in knowledge insufficiency and limited adaptability, which hinder their capacity to perform diagnostic reasoning. Moreover, these methods focus solely on the accuracy of final predictions, overlooking alignment with standard clinical reasoning trajectories. To this end, we propose MultiDx, a two-stage diagnostic reasoning framework that performs differential diagnosis by analyzing evidence collected from multiple knowledge sources. Specifically, it first generates suspected diagnoses and reasoning paths by leveraging knowledge from web search, SOAP-formatted case, and clinical case database. Then it integrates multi-perspective evidence through matching, voting, and differential diagnosis to generate the final prediction.~Extensive experiments on two public benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach.

### [53] [Rewarding the Scientific Process: Process-Level Reward Modeling for Agentic Data Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24198v2)
*Zhisong Qiu,Shuofei Qiao,Kewei Xu,Yuqi Zhu,Lun Du,Ningyu Zhang,Huajun Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 专为agent数据科学设计的过程奖励模型，可检测静默错误，直接适用于代码优化agent的验证。

TL;DR: 提出DataPRM，一种环境感知的过程奖励模型，通过主动验证和三元奖励策略，显著提升数据分析任务的推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用过程奖励模型在动态数据分析任务中无法检测静默错误并误判探索行为，限制了其作为监督者的有效性。

Method: 设计环境感知生成式过程奖励模型DataPRM，包含主动环境交互和反射感知三元奖励；构建超过8K训练实例的流水线。

Result: DataPRM在ScienceAgentBench和DABStep上分别提升7.21%和11.28%，4B参数超越强基线，集成强化学习后达到78.73%和64.84%的准确率。

Conclusion: DataPRM通过过程奖励监督有效提升LLMs在数据分析任务中的推理能力，并泛化到多种测试时缩放策略。

中文摘要：过程奖励模型（PRMs）在静态领域（如数学）中已经取得了显著成功，增强了大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力。然而，它们在动态数据分析任务中的潜力尚未被充分探索。在这项工作中，我们首先通过实证研究发现，通用领域的PRMs难以监督数据分析代理。具体来说，它们无法检测到静默错误（即导致错误结果但不触发解释器异常的逻辑缺陷），并且错误地惩罚探索性行为，将必要的试错探索误判为接地失败。为了弥补这一差距，我们引入了DataPRM，一种新颖的环境感知生成式过程奖励模型，它（1）可以充当主动验证器，自主与环境交互以探查中间执行状态并发现静默错误，以及（2）采用反射感知的三元奖励策略，区分可纠正的接地错误和不可恢复的失误。我们设计了一个可扩展的流水线，通过多样性驱动的轨迹生成和知识增强的步骤级标注，为DataPRM构建了超过8K个高质量训练实例。实验结果表明，使用Best-of-N推理，DataPRM将下游策略LLMs在ScienceAgentBench上的性能提高了7.21%，在DABStep上提高了11.28%。值得注意的是，仅用4B参数，DataPRM就超越了强基线，并在多种测试时缩放策略中展现出强大的泛化能力。此外，将DataPRM集成到强化学习中，相对于结果奖励基线获得了显著提升，在DABench上达到78.73%，在TableBench上达到64.84%，验证了过程奖励监督的有效性。代码可在 https://github.com/zjunlp/DataMind 获取。

Original abstract: Process Reward Models (PRMs) have achieved remarkable success in augmenting the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) within static domains such as mathematics. However, their potential in dynamic data analysis tasks remains underexplored. In this work, we first present a empirical study revealing that general-domain PRMs struggle to supervise data analysis agents. Specifically, they fail to detect silent errors, logical flaws that yield incorrect results without triggering interpreter exceptions, and erroneously penalize exploratory actions, mistaking necessary trial-and-error exploration for grounding failures. To bridge this gap, we introduce DataPRM, a novel environment-aware generative process reward model that (1) can serve as an active verifier, autonomously interacting with the environment to probe intermediate execution states and uncover silent errors, and (2) employs a reflection-aware ternary reward strategy that distinguishes between correctable grounding errors and irrecoverable mistakes. We design a scalable pipeline to construct over 8K high-quality training instances for DataPRM via diversity-driven trajectory generation and knowledge-augmented step-level annotation. Experimental results demonstrate that DataPRM improves downstream policy LLMs by 7.21% on ScienceAgentBench and 11.28% on DABStep using Best-of-N inference. Notably, with only 4B parameters, DataPRM outperforms strong baselines, and exhibits robust generalizability across diverse Test-Time Scaling strategies. Furthermore, integrating DataPRM into Reinforcement Learning yields substantial gains over outcome-reward baselines, achieving 78.73% on DABench and 64.84% on TableBench, validating the effectiveness of process reward supervision. Code is available at https://github.com/zjunlp/DataMind.

### [54] [SeaEvo: Advancing Algorithm Discovery with Strategy Space Evolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24372v2)
*Sichun Luo,Yi Huang,Haochen Luo,Fengyuan Liu,Guanzhi Deng,Lei Li,Qinghua Yao,Zefa Hu,Junlan Feng,Qi Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM引导进化搜索中，策略推理通常是临时或非结构化的，难以区分相似策略、保留低适应度但有前景的方向，或检测策略饱和。

Method: 提出\model，一个模块化策略空间层，将每个候选程序关联一个自然语言策略，按策略语义聚类，检索互补灵感，并定期导航策略景观以避免饱和方向。

Result: 在算法发现、系统优化和智能体框架设计任务中，在大多数设置下改进了现有进化骨架；四个系统基准平均相对改进20.6%，Prism最佳单次运行得分高3倍。

Conclusion: 持久策略表示为提高LLM引导进化搜索的有效性和成本效益提供实用机制，有助于构建通过结构化积累和重用算法策略来增强搜索能力的复合AI系统。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）引导的进化搜索越来越多地被用于自动化算法发现，然而大多数当前方法主要通过可执行程序和标量适应度来跟踪搜索进度。即使通过启发式描述或反思使用自然语言推理，它通常仍然是短暂的变异上下文或非结构化记忆，而不是作为持久化的种群级状态组织成战略方向。因此，进化搜索可能难以区分同一想法的语法不同实现，保留低适应度但具有战略前景的方向，或检测整个策略家族何时已经饱和。我们引入了\model，一个模块化的策略空间层，它将语言级战略推理转化为LLM驱动程序搜索中的一级种群级进化状态。\model为每个候选程序表示一个明确的自然语言策略，通过策略语义对档案进行聚类，检索行为上互补的灵感，并定期导航策略景观以避免饱和方向。在不修改底层进化算法的情况下，\model在大多数设置中改进了算法发现、系统优化和智能体框架设计任务中的现有进化骨架。在四个系统基准测试中，\model实现了20.6%的平均相对改进，Prism上的最佳单次运行得分高出3倍。这些结果表明，持久策略表示为提高LLM引导进化搜索的有效性和成本效益提供了一种实用机制，指向复合AI系统，其搜索能力受益于算法策略的结构化积累和重用。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-guided evolutionary search is increasingly used for automated algorithm discovery, yet most current methods track search progress primarily through executable programs and scalar fitness. Even when natural-language reasoning is used through heuristic descriptions or reflection, it typically remains transient mutation context or unstructured memory, rather than organized as persistent population-level state over strategic directions. As a result, evolutionary search can struggle to distinguish syntactically different implementations of the same idea, preserve lower-fitness but strategically promising directions, or detect when an entire family of strategies has saturated.
  We introduce \model, a modular strategy-space layer that turns language-level strategic reasoning into first-class population-level evolutionary state in LLM-driven program search. \model represents each candidate program with an explicit natural-language strategy, clusters the archive by strategy semantics, retrieves behaviorally complementary inspirations, and periodically navigates the strategy landscape to avoid saturated directions. Without modifying the underlying evolutionary algorithms, \model improves existing evolutionary backbones across algorithm discovery, systems optimization, and agent-scaffold design tasks in most settings. Across four systems benchmarks, \model achieves a 20.6% average relative improvement, with the best single run on Prism scoring 3$\times$ higher. These results suggest that persistent strategy representations provide a practical mechanism for improving the effectiveness and cost-efficiency of LLM-guided evolutionary search, pointing toward compound AI systems whose search capabilities benefit from the structured accumulation and reuse of algorithmic strategies.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图表代码生成主要针对Python，忽略了其他语言（R、LaTeX）中语义等效脚本提供的监督信号。

中文摘要：图表到代码生成将图表图像转换为可执行的绘图脚本，从而实现忠实再现和可编辑的可视化。现有方法主要基于Python，限制了实际应用，并忽略了一个关键的监督来源：相同的图表可以用不同绘图语言中的语义等效脚本表达。为了填补这一空白，我们引入了Chart2NCode数据集，包含176K图表，配对了Python、R和LaTeX中的对齐脚本，这些脚本渲染出视觉等效的输出，通过元数据到模板的流水线构建，并经过渲染验证和人工质量检查。基于LLaVA风格的架构，我们进一步提出了CharLuMA，一种参数高效的适配模块，它用语言条件混合的低秩子空间增强多模态投影器，使模型能够共享核心图表理解，同时通过轻量级路由将代码生成专门化到目标语言。大量实验表明，在所有语言上，可执行性和视觉保真度均持续改进，优于强开源基线，并与专有系统竞争。进一步分析表明，平衡的多语言监督有益于所有语言，适配器分配了一个紧凑的共享核心加上语言特定的容量。代码和数据可在https://github.com/Zhihan72/CharLuMA获取。

Original abstract: Chart-to-code generation converts a chart image into an executable plotting script, enabling faithful reproduction and editable visualizations. Existing methods are largely Python-centric, limiting practical use and overlooking a critical source of supervision: the same chart can be expressed by semantically equivalent scripts in different plotting languages. To fill this gap, we introduce Chart2NCode, a dataset of 176K charts paired with aligned scripts in Python, R, and LaTeX that render visually equivalent outputs, constructed via a metadata-to-template pipeline with rendering verification and human quality checks. Building on a LLaVA-style architecture, we further propose CharLuMA, a parameter-efficient adaptation module that augments the multimodal projector with a language-conditioned mixture of low-rank subspaces, allowing the model to share core chart understanding while specializing code generation to the target language through lightweight routing. Extensive experiments show consistent gains in executability and visual fidelity across all languages, outperforming strong open-source baselines and remaining competitive with proprietary systems. Further analyses reveal that balanced multi-language supervision benefits all languages and that the adapter allocates a compact shared core plus language-specific capacity. Codes and data are available at https://github.com/Zhihan72/CharLuMA.

### [56] [Skill Retrieval Augmentation for Agentic AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24594v3)
*Weihang Su,Jianming Long,Qingyao Ai,Qiaozhi He,Yichen Tang,Changyue Wang,Yiteng Tu,Yingbo Wang,Yiqun Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出技能检索增强范式SRA，直接提升agent技能应用能力，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 本文提出技能检索增强（SRA）范式，让LLM智能体按需从大技能库中动态检索并应用技能；构建了SRA-Bench基准，发现技能融入是当前瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体系统在上下文中枚举技能的策略无法扩展，导致上下文预算耗尽和技能识别准确率下降。

Method: 构建大规模技能语料库（26,262个技能）和SRA-Bench基准（5,400个测试实例、636个金标准技能），通过检索增强技能，并评估检索、融入和任务执行全流程。

Result: 检索增强显著提升智能体性能，但发现LLM在技能融入上存在瓶颈：无论是否检索到相关技能，加载行为相似。

Conclusion: 技能增强的瓶颈既在检索也在融入，SRA成为独立研究问题，为未来可扩展能力增强奠定基础。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型（LLM）演变为智能体问题求解器，它们越来越依赖外部的、可复用的技能来处理超出其原生参数能力的任务。在现有的智能体系统中，融入技能的主要策略是在上下文窗口中显式枚举可用技能。然而，这种策略无法扩展：随着技能库的扩大，上下文预算迅速消耗，智能体在识别正确技能方面的准确性显著下降。为此，本文提出了技能检索增强（SRA），这是一种新的范式，其中智能体按需从大型外部技能库中动态检索、融入并应用相关技能。为了使该问题可测量，我们构建了一个大规模技能库，并引入了SRA-Bench，这是第一个用于全面评估完整SRA流程（涵盖技能检索、技能融入和最终任务执行）的基准。SRA-Bench包含5,400个能力密集型测试实例和636个人工构建的金标准技能，这些与从网络收集的干扰技能混合，形成一个包含26,262个技能的大规模语料库。大量实验表明，基于检索的技能增强可以显著提高智能体性能，验证了这一范式的潜力。同时，我们发现了技能融入中的一个基本差距：当前的LLM智能体倾向于以相似的速率加载技能，无论是否检索到了金标准技能，或者任务是否实际需要外部能力。这表明技能增强的瓶颈不仅在于检索，还在于基础模型判断加载哪个技能以及何时实际需要外部加载的能力。这些发现将SRA定位为一个独特的研究问题，并为未来智能体系统中能力的可扩展增强奠定了基础。

Original abstract: As large language models (LLMs) evolve into agentic problem solvers, they increasingly rely on external, reusable skills to handle tasks beyond their native parametric capabilities. In existing agent systems, the dominant strategy for incorporating skills is to explicitly enumerate available skills within the context window. However, this strategy fails to scale: as skill corpora expand, context budgets are consumed rapidly, and the agent becomes markedly less accurate in identifying the right skill. To this end, this paper formulates Skill Retrieval Augmentation (SRA), a new paradigm in which agents dynamically retrieve, incorporate, and apply relevant skills from large external skill corpora on demand. To make this problem measurable, we construct a large-scale skill corpus and introduce SRA-Bench, the first benchmark for decomposed evaluation of the full SRA pipeline, covering skill retrieval, skill incorporation, and end-task execution. SRA-Bench contains 5,400 capability-intensive test instances and 636 manually constructed gold skills, which are mixed with web-collected distractor skills to form a large-scale corpus of 26,262 skills. Extensive experiments show that retrieval-based skill augmentation can substantially improve agent performance, validating the promise of the paradigm. At the same time, we uncover a fundamental gap in skill incorporation: current LLM agents tend to load skills at similar rates, regardless of whether a gold skill is retrieved or whether the task actually requires external capabilities. This shows that the bottleneck in skill augmentation lies not only in retrieval but also in the base model's ability to determine which skill to load and when external loading is actually needed. These findings position SRA as a distinct research problem and establish a foundation for the scalable augmentation of capabilities in future agent systems.

</details>


### [57] [Less is More: Lightweight Prompt Compression for Question Answering Applications on Edge Devices](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20571v1)
*Zihuai Xu,Ruofei Hou,Yang Xu,Hongli Xu,Yunming Liao,Ying Zhu*
