TL;DR: CORE是一种无需小语言模型的两阶段句子级提示压缩方法，通过NER和语义匹配构建答案集和线索集，再通过正交残差检索和空间邻近度过滤进行优化，在边缘设备上显著提升准确率、减少内存和能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示压缩方法依赖辅助小语言模型（SLM）导致计算和内存开销大，不适合资源受限的边缘设备。

Method: CORE：第一阶段通过NER构建答案集，通过语义匹配构建线索集；第二阶段使用正交残差检索精炼线索集，基于空间邻近度度量过滤答案集，合并两集合得到压缩上下文。

Result: 在2000 token预算下，CORE相比SOTA准确率提升至少30.19%，内存减少至少50.47%，边缘设备加速至少1.94倍，智能手机能耗降低95.74%。

Conclusion: CORE在边缘设备上实现了高效且准确的提示压缩，无需额外小语言模型，具有实用性和泛化能力，适合移动部署。

中文摘要：在智能体驱动的问答（QA）应用中，检索增强生成（RAG）通常被引入以通过提供额外上下文来增强大语言模型（LLM）的响应准确性。由于检索结果中固有的噪声以及文档级检索的粗粒度，检索到的上下文通常包含大量冗余信息。在这种设置下，由用户查询和关联检索上下文组成的智能体提示会导致LLM推理期间产生不必要的计算开销。现有的提示压缩方法通常依赖辅助小语言模型（SLM）来估计上下文重要性。然而，这些方法会引入显著的内存和计算开销，限制了它们在资源受限的边缘设备上的部署。本文提出CORE，一种无需SLM的两阶段句子级提示压缩方法。在第一阶段，CORE通过命名实体识别（NER）构建答案集，并通过语义匹配构建线索集。在第二阶段，CORE使用正交残差检索策略精炼线索集，并设计基于空间邻近度的度量来过滤答案集。然后将两个集合合并形成最终的压缩上下文。我们在NVIDIA Jetson AGX Orin边缘设备和华为Nova智能手机上实现CORE。实验结果表明，在2000个token的预算内，CORE相较于最先进的基线方法，准确率至少提升30.19%，内存使用至少减少50.47%，并且在边缘设备上实现至少1.94倍的加速。此外，与最先进的LLMLingua2方法相比，CORE在智能手机上实现了95.74%的大幅能耗降低，突显了其在移动部署中的实用性和泛化能力。

Original abstract: In agent-driven question answering (QA) applications, retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) is commonly introduced to enhance the response accuracy of large language models (LLMs) by providing additional context. Due to the inherent noise in retrieval results and the coarse granularity of document-level retrieval, the retrieved context often contains substantial redundant information. In this setting, the agent prompt, consisting of the user query and the associated retrieved context, leads to unnecessary computational overhead during LLM inference. Existing prompt compression methods typically rely on auxiliary small language models (SLMs) to estimate context importance. However, such approaches introduce significant memory and computational overhead, which limits their deployment on resource-constrained edge devices. In this paper, we propose CORE, a two-stage sentence-level prompt compression method that eliminates the need for SLMs. In the first stage, CORE constructs an answer set via named entity recognition (NER) and a clue set via semantic matching. In the second stage, CORE refines the clue set using an orthogonal residual retrieval strategy and designs a spatial proximity-based metric to filter the answer set. The two sets are then combined to form the final compressed context. We implement CORE on an NVIDIA Jetson AGX Orin edge device and a Huawei Nova smartphone. Experimental results demonstrate that within a 2000-token budget, CORE improves accuracy by at least 30.19% compared to state-of-the-art baselines, while reducing memory usage by at least 50.47% and achieving at least 1.94 times speedup on the edge device. Moreover, compared to the state-of-the-art LLMLingua2 method, CORE achieves a substantial energy reduction of 95.74% on the smartphone, highlighting its practicality and generalizability for mobile deployments.

</details>


### [58] [Green Shielding: A User-Centric Approach Towards Trustworthy AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24700v1)
*Aaron J. Li,Nicolas Sanchez,Hao Huang,Ruijiang Dong,Jaskaran Bains,Katrin Jaradeh,Zhen Xiang,Bo Li,Feng Liu,Aaron Kornblith,Bin Yu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 用户视角的AI信任框架，虽专注医疗但宣称可扩展至agent系统，对agent鲁棒性评估有一般启发。

TL;DR: 提出绿色屏蔽议程，通过CUE标准与PCS框架，在医疗诊断中构建基准HCM-Dx，研究常规输入变化对LLM输出的影响，发现中性化等扰动会带来临床相关的权衡，支持用户指南以提升高风险领域部署安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有红队测试未充分解决LLM输出对用户查询常规非对抗性变化的敏感性，需要建立以用户为中心的部署指南。

Method: 提出绿色屏蔽议程，操作化为CUE标准（真实语境、效用指标、现实扰动），结合PCS框架，与医师合作构建HCM-Dx基准（患者查询、参考诊断集、临床指标），并研究多种提示层面扰动。

Result: 提示层面因素系统性地改变模型行为；中性化增加合理性和简洁性，但降低高概率和安全关键条件的覆盖，呈现帕累托式权衡。

Conclusion: 交互选择可系统影响模型输出任务相关属性，支持用户指南以促进高风险领域安全部署，议程可推广至其他决策支持系统。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的部署日益增多，但其输出可能对用户在查询措辞中的常规、非对抗性变化高度敏感，现有红队测试工作未能很好地解决这一问题。我们提出“绿色屏蔽”（Green Shielding），这是一个以用户为中心的议程，旨在通过描述良性输入变化如何改变模型行为，来构建基于证据的部署指南。我们通过CUE标准来操作化这一议程：具有真实语境的基准测试、参考标准和捕捉真实效用的指标，以及反映模型行为引出中现实变化的扰动。在PCS框架指导下，并与执业医师合作，我们在医疗诊断中实例化绿色屏蔽，通过HealthCareMagic-Diagnosis（HCM-Dx）——一个由患者撰写的查询基准，以及结构化的参考诊断集和用于评估鉴别诊断列表的临床客观指标。我们还研究了捕捉常规输入变化的扰动机制，并表明提示层面因素沿着临床有意义的维度改变模型行为。在多个前沿LLM上，这些变化描绘出类似帕累托的权衡。特别是，中性化（neutralization）在保留临床内容的同时移除了常见的用户层面因素，增加了合理性并产生了更简洁、类似临床医生的鉴别诊断，但降低了对高概率和安全关键条件的覆盖。总之，这些结果表明交互选择可以系统地改变模型输出的任务相关属性，并支持面向用户的指南，以在高风险领域实现更安全的部署。虽然在此实例化为医疗诊断，但该议程自然扩展到其他决策支持场景和代理型AI系统。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed, yet their outputs can be highly sensitive to routine, non-adversarial variation in how users phrase queries, a gap not well addressed by existing red-teaming efforts. We propose Green Shielding, a user-centric agenda for building evidence-backed deployment guidance by characterizing how benign input variation shifts model behavior. We operationalize this agenda through the CUE criteria: benchmarks with authentic Context, reference standards and metrics that capture true Utility, and perturbations that reflect realistic variations in the Elicitation of model behavior. Guided by the PCS framework and developed with practicing physicians, we instantiate Green Shielding in medical diagnosis through HealthCareMagic-Diagnosis (HCM-Dx), a benchmark of patient-authored queries, together with structured reference diagnosis sets and clinically grounded metrics for evaluating differential diagnosis lists. We also study perturbation regimes that capture routine input variation and show that prompt-level factors shift model behavior along clinically meaningful dimensions. Across multiple frontier LLMs, these shifts trace out Pareto-like tradeoffs. In particular, neutralization, which removes common user-level factors while preserving clinical content, increases plausibility and yields more concise, clinician-like differentials, but reduces coverage of highly likely and safety-critical conditions. Together, these results show that interaction choices can systematically shift task-relevant properties of model outputs and support user-facing guidance for safer deployment in high-stakes domains. Although instantiated here in medical diagnosis, the agenda extends naturally to other decision-support settings and agentic AI systems.

</details>


### [59] [Large Language Models Explore by Latent Distilling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24927v1)
*Yuanhao Zeng,Ao Lu,Lufei Li,Zheng Zhang,Yexin Li,Kan Ren*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 探索性采样方法提升LLM语义多样性，可迁移至agent探索策略。

TL;DR: 提出ESamp解码方法，通过训练轻量级蒸馏器预测LLM深层表示，利用预测误差作为新颖性信号重新加权候选词元，从而提升生成语义多样性和推理模型的Pass@k效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准随机采样仅产生表面词汇变化，限制语义探索，而神经网络对新颖输入预测误差较高的特性可用于鼓励语义多样性。

Method: 在测试时训练轻量级蒸馏器，从LLM浅层表示预测深层表示，建模深度方向表示转换；解码时蒸馏器不断适应上下文，利用预测误差作为新颖性信号重新加权候选词元，偏向较少探索的语义模式；使用异步训练-推理流水线降低开销。

Result: ESamp显著提升推理模型的Pass@k效率，性能优于或媲美强基线，在数学、科学和代码生成基准上泛化良好，并打破创意写作中多样性与连贯性的权衡，开销小于5%（优化版1.2%）。

Conclusion: ESamp是一种有效的解码方法，能在不牺牲连贯性的前提下显著提高生成语义多样性，适用于多种任务，且实现高效。

中文摘要：生成多样化的响应对于大规模语言模型（LLMs）的测试时扩展至关重要，然而标准的随机采样主要产生表面层面的词汇变化，限制了语义探索。在本文中，我们提出探索性采样（ESamp），一种在生成过程中明确鼓励语义多样性的解码方法。ESamp的动机源于一个众所周知的观察：神经网络倾向于对与先前遇到过的输入相似的输入做出较低误差的预测，而对新奇的输入则产生较高的预测误差。基于这一特性，我们在测试时训练一个轻量级的蒸馏器（Distiller），从LLM的浅层表示预测其深层隐藏表示，以建模LLM的深度方向表示转换。在解码过程中，蒸馏器不断适应当前生成上下文所引发的映射。ESamp使用预测误差作为新颖性信号，根据当前前缀对候选词元扩展进行重新加权，从而将解码偏向于较少探索的语义模式。ESamp通过异步训练-推理流水线实现，最坏情况下的开销小于5%（优化版本为1.2%）。实验结果表明，ESamp显著提升了推理模型的Pass@k效率，在性能上优于或可与强随机和启发式基线相媲美。值得注意的是，ESamp在数学、科学和代码生成基准测试中展现出稳健的泛化能力，并在创意写作中打破了多样性与连贯性之间的权衡。我们的代码已发布在：https://github.com/LinesHogan/tLLM。

Original abstract: Generating diverse responses is crucial for test-time scaling of large language models (LLMs), yet standard stochastic sampling mostly yields surface-level lexical variation, limiting semantic exploration. In this paper, we propose Exploratory Sampling (ESamp), a decoding approach that explicitly encourages semantic diversity during generation. ESamp is motivated by the well-known observation that neural networks tend to make lower-error predictions on inputs similar to those encountered before, and incur higher prediction error on novel ones. Building on this property, we train a lightweight Distiller at test time to predict deep-layer hidden representations of the LLM from its shallow-layer representations to model the LLM's depth-wise representation transitions. During decoding, the Distiller continuously adapts to the mappings induced by the current generation context. ESamp uses the prediction error as a novelty signal to reweight candidate token extensions conditioned on the current prefix, thereby biasing decoding toward less-explored semantic patterns. ESamp is implemented with an asynchronous training--inference pipeline, with less than 5% worst case overhead (1.2% in the optimized release). Empirical results show that ESamp significantly boosts the Pass@k efficiency of reasoning models, showing superior or comparable performance to strong stochastic and heuristic baselines. Notably, ESamp achieves robust generalization across mathematics, science, and code generation benchmarks and breaks the trade-off between diversity and coherence in creative writing. Our code has released at: https://github.com/LinesHogan/tLLM.

</details>


### [60] [GAIA-v2-LILT: Multilingual Adaptation of Agent Benchmark beyond Translation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24929v1)
*Yunsu Kim,Kaden Uhlig,Joern Wuebker*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: GAIA agent benchmark的多语言适配，直接相关agent评测与方法。

TL;DR: 提出一种精炼的多语言agent基准工作流，通过功能、文化和难度校准，显著提升性能，并揭示了大部分多语言差距源于基准测量误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通过机器翻译和有限后期编辑构建多语言agent基准，导致查询-答案不对齐和文化不相关，破坏基准有效性。

Method: 提出精炼工作流，包括显式功能对齐、文化对齐和难度校准，结合自动检查与人工审核，将英语基准适应到多种语言。

Result: 工作流使agent成功率相比最小翻译版本提升高达32.7%，最佳审计设置下性能差距缩小至3.1%，但多数语言仍存在显著差距。

Conclusion: 多语言性能差距主要由基准引起的测量误差导致，建议在跨语言适应时进行任务级对齐。

中文摘要：Agent基准测试在很大程度上仍然以英语为中心，而其多语言版本通常通过机器翻译（MT）和有限的后期编辑构建。我们认为，对于agent任务，这种最小工作流很容易通过查询-答案不对齐或文化上不相关的上下文破坏基准的有效性。我们提出了一种精炼的工作流，用于将英语基准测试适应到多种语言，通过自动检查和人工审核，实现显式的功能对齐、文化对齐和难度校准。使用此工作流，我们推出了GAIA-v2-LILT，这是GAIA的重新审计的多语言扩展，涵盖五种非英语语言。在实验中，我们的工作流相对于最小翻译版本将agent成功率提高了高达32.7%，使最接近审计设置的结果在英语性能的3.1%以内，但在许多其他情况下仍存在显著差距。这表明，多语言性能差距的很大一部分是基准引起的测量误差，这激发了在跨语言适应英语基准时进行任务级对齐。该数据作为MAPS包的一部分，可在https://huggingface.co/datasets/Fujitsu-FRE/MAPS/viewer/GAIA-v2-LILT获取。我们还发布了实验中使用的代码：https://github.com/lilt/gaia-v2-lilt。

Original abstract: Agent benchmarks remain largely English-centric, while their multilingual versions are often built with machine translation (MT) and limited post-editing. We argue that, for agentic tasks, this minimal workflow can easily break benchmark validity through query-answer misalignment or culturally off-target context. We propose a refined workflow for adapting English benchmarks into multiple languages with explicit functional alignment, cultural alignment, and difficulty calibration using both automated checks and human review. Using this workflow, we introduce GAIA-v2-LILT, a re-audited multilingual extension of GAIA covering five non-English languages. In experiments, our workflow improves agent success rates by up to 32.7% over minimally translated versions, bringing the closest audited setting to within 3.1% of English performance while substantial gaps remain in many other cases. This indicates that a substantial share of the multilingual performance gap is benchmark-induced measurement error, motivating task-level alignment when adapting English benchmarks across languages. The data is available as part of the MAPS package at https://huggingface.co/datasets/Fujitsu-FRE/MAPS/viewer/GAIA-v2-LILT. We also release the code used in our experiments at https://github.com/lilt/gaia-v2-lilt.

### [61] [BenchGuard: Who Guards the Benchmarks? Automated Auditing of LLM Agent Benchmarks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24955v1)
*Xinming Tu,Tianze Wang,Yingzhou,Lu,Kexin Huang,Yuanhao Qu,Sara Mostafavi*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了BenchGuard，首个自动化审计框架，用于检测基于任务的智能体基准测试中的缺陷，在科学基准测试中发现了被忽视的错误，成本低且效果显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多智能体失败实际上是基准测试本身的缺陷（如糟糕的规范、隐含假设、僵化脚本），而非智能体问题，因此需要系统性的审计方法。

Method: 利用前沿大语言模型作为审计者，通过结构化协议交叉验证基准测试的所有组成部分，并可选地使用智能体解决方案或执行轨迹作为额外证据。

Result: 在ScienceAgentBench发现12个作者确认的问题（包括致命错误），在BIXBench Verified-50子集匹配83.3%的专家识别问题，且全审计成本低于15美元。

Conclusion: 自动化基准测试审计是可行且实用的，前沿模型应作为评估基础设施的验证者而非仅作为评估对象，推动AI辅助基准测试开发。

中文摘要：随着基准测试变得越来越复杂，许多表面上智能体的失败并非智能体本身的失败——而是基准测试本身的失败：糟糕的规范、隐含的假设以及惩罚有效替代方法的僵化评估脚本。我们提出利用前沿大语言模型作为评估基础设施的系统性审计者，并通过BenchGuard实现这一愿景，这是首个面向任务导向、基于执行的智能体基准测试的自动化审计框架。BenchGuard通过结构化大语言模型协议交叉验证所有基准测试产物，并可选择性地引入智能体解决方案或执行轨迹作为额外诊断证据。在两个著名的科学基准测试上，BenchGuard在ScienceAgentBench中发现了12个经作者确认的问题——包括导致任务无法解决的致命错误——并且在BIXBench Verified-50子集上精确匹配了83.3%的专家识别问题，捕捉到了此前人工审查完全遗漏的缺陷。对50个复杂生物信息学任务进行完整审计的成本低于15美元，使得自动化基准测试审计成为人工审查的实用且有价值的补充。这些发现指向了AI辅助的基准测试开发，其中前沿模型不仅作为评估对象，而且作为验证评估基础设施本身的积极参与者。

Original abstract: As benchmarks grow in complexity, many apparent agent failures are not failures of the agent at all - they are failures of the benchmark itself: broken specifications, implicit assumptions, and rigid evaluation scripts that penalize valid alternative approaches. We propose employing frontier LLMs as systematic auditors of evaluation infrastructure, and realize this vision through BenchGuard, the first automated auditing framework for task-oriented, execution-based agent benchmarks. BenchGuard cross-verifies all benchmark artifacts via structured LLM protocols, optionally incorporating agent solutions or execution traces as additional diagnostic evidence. Deployed on two prominent scientific benchmarks, BenchGuard identified 12 author-confirmed issues in ScienceAgentBench - including fatal errors rendering tasks unsolvable - and exactly matched 83.3% of expert-identified issues on the BIXBench Verified-50 subset, catching defects that prior human review missed entirely. A full audit of 50 complex bioinformatics tasks costs under USD 15, making automated benchmark auditing a practical and valuable complement to human review. These findings point toward AI-assisted benchmark development, where frontier models serve not only as subjects of evaluation but as active participants in validating the evaluation infrastructure itself.

### [62] [Dont Stop Early: Scalable Enterprise Deep Research with Controlled Information Flow and Evidence-Aware Termination](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24978v1)
*Prafulla Kumar Choubey,Kung-Hsiang Huang,Pranav Narayanan Venkit,Jiaxin Zhang,Vaibhav Vats,Yu Li,Xiangyu Peng,Chien-Sheng Wu*

TL;DR: 提出EDR架构，通过分解目标、定位上下文和基于证据的完成标准，减少过早停止，提高企业研究的深度和一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业深度研究因信息覆盖不均衡、上下文爆炸和过早停止而失败，需要更可靠的架构。

Method: 使用提纲生成与反思分解请求、依赖引导的执行定位上下文、基于证据的完成标准确保信息充分性。

Result: 在内部销售赋能任务和DeepResearch Bench基准上取得最佳性能，减少了过早停止。

Conclusion: 依赖控制的上下文和证据充分性标准显著提高了企业研究的一致性和深度。

中文摘要：企业深度研究往往由于信息覆盖不均衡、上下文爆炸和过早停止而无法产生可用于决策的报告。我们提出了一种可扩展的企业深度研究（EDR）架构来解决这些问题。我们的系统（i）通过带有反思的提纲生成将请求分解为覆盖驱动的目标，（ii）通过依赖引导的执行和显式信息共享来定位上下文，以及（iii）实施基于证据的完成标准，使得智能体迭代收集信息直到满足充分性条件。我们在一个内部销售赋能任务和公共DeepResearch Bench基准上进行了评估，我们提出的系统设计在性能上相较于有竞争力的深度研究基线取得了最强的整体表现。结果表明，依赖控制的上下文和显式的证据充分性标准减少了过早停止，并提高了企业研究输出的一致性和深度。

Original abstract: Enterprise deep research often fails to produce decision-ready reports due to uneven information coverage, context explosion, and premature stopping. We propose a scalable Enterprise Deep Research (EDR) architecture to address these failures. Our system (i) decomposes requests into coverage-driven objectives via outline generation with reflection, (ii) localizes context with dependency-guided execution and explicit information sharing, and (iii) enforces evidence-based completion criteria so agents iteratively collect information until sufficiency conditions are met. We evaluate on an internal sales enablement task and the public DeepResearch Bench benchmark, where our proposed system design achieves the strongest overall performance compared with competitive deep-research baselines. The results show that dependency-controlled context and explicit evidence sufficiency criteria reduce premature stopping and improve the consistency and depth of enterprise research outputs.

</details>


### [63] [Faithful Autoformalization via Roundtrip Verification and Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25031v2)
*Daneshvar Amrollahi,Jerry Lopez,Clark Barrett*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM自动形式化验证与修复，验证方法可迁移到coding agent

TL;DR: 提出一种基于往返验证的大语言模型形式化忠实性检查方法，通过诊断引导的修复提高一致性，并在法规领域验证有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏自动验证大语言模型形式化输出忠实性的方法，需要无需地面真值标注的可靠途径。

Method: 采用往返验证框架：先形式化自然语言陈述，再翻译回自然语言，重新形式化，用形式化工具检查逻辑等价性；当不一致时，通过阶段级诊断定位错误步骤，并应用范围限定修复算子纠正。

Result: 诊断引导的范围限定修复是最有效的方法；未通过等价性检查的规则比通过的规则显示1.4-2.5倍更多的NLI漂移。

Conclusion: 往返验证结合诊断引导修复能有效检测并修复不忠实的形式化，且失败规则的NLI漂移更高佐证了方法的区分能力。

中文摘要：当大语言模型将自然语言形式化时，我们如何知道输出是忠实的？我们提出了一种往返验证方法，不需要地面真值标注：形式化一个陈述，将结果翻译回自然语言，重新形式化，并使用形式化工具检查逻辑等价性。当两个形式化结果一致时，这提供了忠实形式化的证据。当它们不一致时，阶段级诊断将错误定位到特定的翻译步骤，然后一个范围限定修复算子尝试纠正该步骤。我们使用两个大语言模型（Claude Opus~4.6和GPT-5.2）在两个法规领域（德克萨斯州交通法规和德克萨斯州公园与野生动物法规）上评估了该框架，并使用了三种修复基线。诊断引导的范围限定修复是最有效的方法，其有效性取决于诊断函数的可靠性。在两个领域和两个模型上，在我们的完整修复系统下，未通过等价性检查的规则比通过的规则显示出1.4倍到2.5倍更多的NLI漂移。

Original abstract: When an LLM formalizes natural language, how do we know the output is faithful? We propose a roundtrip verification approach which does not require ground-truth annotations: formalize a statement, translate the result back to natural language, re-formalize, and use a formal tool to check logical equivalence. When the two formalizations agree, this provides evidence of a faithful formalization. When they disagree, a stage-level diagnosis localizes the error to a specific translation step, and a scoped repair operator attempts to correct that step. We evaluate the framework on two statutory domains (the Texas Transportation Code and the Texas Parks and Wildlife Code) using two LLMs (Claude Opus~4.6 and GPT-5.2) with three repair baselines. Diagnosis-guided scoped repair is the most effective method, with effectiveness contingent on the reliability of the diagnosis function. Across both domains and both models, under our full repair system, rules that fail the equivalence check show 1.4x-2.5x more NLI drift than rules that pass it.

</details>


### [64] [Dual-Track CoT: Budget-Aware Stepwise Guidance for Small LMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25039v1)
*Sagnik Chatterjee,Atharva Patil,Sricharan Ramesh*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 预算感知的CoT推理，为agent规划提供效率控制启发

TL;DR: 该项目研究小语言模型（SLM）在严格令牌预算下通过过程监督和简单测试时控制实现可靠的多步推理，以替代大模型或大量采样。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM推理方法在小模型上成本高且缺乏步骤级控制，而实际部署（如设备端）需要低成本高效率的推理。

Method: 通过过程监督、令牌预算控制和拒绝冗余步骤等简单测试时控制策略来提升SLM推理性能。

Result: 未在摘要中提供具体实验结果，但预期能提高SLM在固定成本下的推理可靠性。

Conclusion: 该方法有望在不增加模型规模或采样次数的情况下，让SLM实现可靠的推理，适用于资源受限场景。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）通过思维链（CoT）提示解决许多推理任务，但较小的模型（约7到8B参数）在严格的计算和令牌预算下仍然难以进行多步推理。现有的测试时推理方法，如自一致性（对多个推理过程进行采样并投票）、思维树（对中间思维进行搜索）和批判修正循环，虽然提高了性能，但通常令牌成本高且缺乏细粒度的步骤级控制。本项目旨在解决这一差距：小语言模型（SLM）能否使用相同或更少的令牌可靠地进行推理？这个问题既具有科学性又具有实践性。从科学上讲，它探究了过程监督和简单的测试时控制（如令牌预算和拒绝冗余步骤）是否可以替代模型规模或大量采样数量。从实践上讲，许多部署（设备端、低延迟或成本受限的环境）无法承受巨大的模型或每次查询数十个采样的推理过程。因此，一种在固定成本下提高SLM推理性能的方法将直接有用。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) solve many reasoning tasks via chain-of-thought (CoT) prompting, but smaller models (about 7 to 8B parameters) still struggle with multi-step reasoning under tight compute and token budgets. Existing test time reasoning methods such as self consistency (sampling multiple rationales and voting), Tree-of-Thoughts (search over intermediate thoughts), and critique revise loops improve performance, but often at high token cost and without fine-grained step-level control. This project1 aims to address that gap: can Small Language Models (SLMs) reason reliably using the same or fewer tokens? This question is both scientific and practical. Scientifically, it probes whether process supervision and simple test-time controls (such as token budgets and rejection of redundant steps) can substitute for model scale or large sampling counts. Practically, many deployments (on-device, low-latency, or cost-constrained settings) cannot afford huge models or dozens of sampled rationales per query. A method that improves SLM reasoning at fixed cost would therefore be directly useful.

</details>

### [65] [Strategic Bidding in 6G Spectrum Auctions with Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24156v1)
*Ismail Lotfi,Ali Ghrayeb*

Main category: cs.GT

Selection reason: LLM作为投标agent在拍卖中自适应，对agent行为设计有启发

TL;DR: 本文首次系统评估了大型语言模型作为竞标代理在重复6G频谱拍卖中的表现，表明在预算约束下LLM能适应并超越传统机制设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决6G网络中频谱分配的高效性和公平性问题，探索LLM作为竞标代理在复杂约束下的策略行为。

Method: 利用LLM作为竞标代理，在重复VCG拍卖中与诚实和启发式策略对比，通过历史结果和提示推理动态调整出价。

Result: 在理论假设成立时LLM恢复近均衡结果；在预算约束下LLM维持更长参与时间并获得更高效用。

Conclusion: LLM竞标者能逼近自适应均衡，对6G网络的市场动态有重塑潜力。

中文摘要：高效且公平的频谱分配是6G网络中的一个核心挑战，其中海量连接和异构服务持续竞争有限的无线电资源。我们研究了在车载网络的具有预算约束的重复6G频谱拍卖中，使用大型语言模型（LLM）作为竞标代理的情况。每个用户设备（UE）作为一个理性参与者，通过重复交互优化其长期效用。以Vickrey-Clarke-Groves（VCG）机制作为激励兼容、占优策略诚实性的基准，我们比较了LLM引导的出价与诚实策略和启发式策略。与启发式不同，LLM利用历史结果和基于提示的推理动态调整其出价行为。结果表明，当保证诚实性的理论假设成立时，LLM竞标者恢复出与VCG预测一致的近均衡结果。然而，当这些假设被打破时——例如在静态预算约束下——LLM能够维持更长的参与时间并获得更高的效用，揭示了它们近似自适应均衡的能力，超越了静态机制设计。这项工作首次系统评估了重复频谱拍卖中的LLM竞标者，为AI驱动代理如何在未来6G网络中战略互动并重塑市场动态提供了新见解。

Original abstract: Efficient and fair spectrum allocation is a central challenge in 6G networks, where massive connectivity and heterogeneous services continuously compete for limited radio resources. We investigate the use of Large Language Models (LLMs) as bidding agents in repeated 6G spectrum auctions with budget constraints in vehicular networks. Each user equipment (UE) acts as a rational player optimizing its long-term utility through repeated interactions. Using the Vickrey-Clarke-Groves (VCG) mechanism as a benchmark for incentive-compatible, dominant-strategy truthfulness, we compare LLM-guided bidding against truthful and heuristic strategies. Unlike heuristics, LLMs leverage historical outcomes and prompt-based reasoning to adapt their bidding behavior dynamically. Results show that when the theoretical assumptions guaranteeing truthfulness hold, LLM bidders recover near-equilibrium outcomes consistent with VCG predictions. However, when these assumptions break -- such as under static budget constraints -- LLMs sustain longer participation and achieve higher utilities, revealing their ability to approximate adaptive equilibria beyond static mechanism design. This work provides the first systematic evaluation of LLM bidders in repeated spectrum auctions, offering new insights into how AI-driven agents can interact strategically and reshape market dynamics in future 6G networks.

</details>

### [66] [Putting a Face to the Issue: Fostering User Empathy of Open Source Software Developers With PersonaFlow](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24478v1)
*Boniface Bahati Tadjuidje,Jin L. C. Guo,Jinghui Cheng*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: PersonaFlow通过生成可编辑用户画像并集成到问题报告中，帮助OSS开发者更好地理解用户，从而改变其回应行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: OSS开发者难以理解用户背景，现有工具侧重技术讨论，用户画像难以规模化。

Method: 开发了PersonaFlow工具，在13名OSS开发者中进行用户研究。

Result: 多数开发者理解用户方式转变，超过一半修改回复，发现了情感连接和实用主义两条路径。

Conclusion: 基于用户画像的工具能提升用户中心行为，为效率驱动系统提供设计启示。

中文摘要：开源软件（OSS）开发者常常难以理解和回应用户背景，而现有工具（如用于处理错误、请求和反馈的问题追踪器）主要关注技术讨论。虽然用户画像可能有所帮助，但有限的资源和用户体验专业知识使其难以规模化。我们提出了PersonaFlow，一个从OSS仓库工件中生成可编辑的用户画像并将其与问题报告集成的工具。在一项包含13名OSS开发者的用户研究中，大多数开发者报告他们对用户的理解发生了转变，超过一半的开发者通过添加共情语言、调整解释或提高优先级评级来修改他们的回复。我们发现了实现这种变化的两种途径：一些人在情感上将用户画像视为真人，而另一些人则将其用于实用主义的分类。两者似乎都导致了更加以用户为中心的行为。我们为基于用户画像的工具提供了设计启示，这些启示适用于OSS以及其他效率驱动系统或工作流程掩盖了宝贵人文因素的场景。

Original abstract: Open-source software (OSS) developers often struggle to understand and respond to user context, while existing tools, such as issue trackers (for handling bugs, requests, and feedback), largely focus on technical discussion. Although personas could help, limited resources and UX expertise make them hard to scale. We present PersonaFlow, a tool that generates editable user personas from OSS repository artifacts and integrates them alongside issue reports. In a user study with 13 OSS developers, most reported shifts in how they understood users, and more than half modified their responses by adding empathetic language, tailoring explanations, or raising priority ratings. We found two pathways to this change: some connected emotionally to personas as people, while others used them pragmatically for triaging. Both appeared to lead to more user-centered behavior. We contribute design implications for persona-based tools relevant to OSS and other contexts where efficiency-driven systems or workflows obscure valuable human elements.

</details>


### [67] [What If We Work Together? Fostering Reflections on Designer Inclusion in Open Source Software Through Speculative Design](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24981v1)
*Rozhan Hozhabri Nezhad,Jin L. C. Guo,Jinghui Cheng*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 使用思辨设计构建两个假想社会（集体主义Husia和个人主义Reetar），通过12名OSS从业者的用户研究，激发了关于设计师包容性和OSS价值观的深刻反思。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: OSS中设计专业知识缺乏和开发者中心思维导致可用性差，限制非技术用户采用，需转变社区观念。

Method: 分析在线论坛了解设计师的动机和挑战，设计两个思辨社会（Husia和Reetar），通过12名OSS从业者（7设计师+5开发者）的用户研究进行评估。

Result: 思辨社会引发了参与者对OSS价值观、挑战根本原因和行动建议的丰富而深刻的反思。

Conclusion: 思辨设计可在实际OSS环境中有效激发批判性反思并提高意识，为构建公平、可持续、包容的OSS环境提供建议。

中文摘要：开源软件（OSS）通常优先考虑技术功能而非可用性和用户体验设计。这种不平衡限制了OSS在更广泛的非技术用户中的采用。导致这一问题的关键潜在因素包括OSS中设计专业知识的缺乏以及以开发者为中心的思维方式。为了解决这些长期存在的问题，我们探索了思辨设计作为催化OSS社区向更包容设计师的环境转变的潜力。我们的设计基于对在线论坛的分析，这些分析揭示了设计师在贡献OSS时的动机和挑战。在这些见解的指导下，我们创建了两个思辨社会：Husia（集体主义）和Reetar（个人主义），在这些社会中，设计师因不同原因受到重视，其工作以不同方式被融入。通过一项涉及12名OSS从业者（7名设计师和5名开发者）的用户研究，我们发现我们的思辨社会引发了参与者对OSS价值观、挑战的根本原因以及拟议行动的丰富而深刻的反思。我们的工作提供了关于如何在实际的、社会技术的OSS环境中使用思辨设计来激发批判性反思、提高意识，并为培育一个公平、可持续和包容的OSS环境提出建议的见解。

Original abstract: Open source software (OSS) often prioritizes technical functionality over usability and UX design. This imbalance limits OSS adoption among broader, non-technical users. Key underlying factors contributing to this issue are the shortage of design expertise in OSS and a dominant developer-centric mindset. To address these persistent issues, we explore the potential of speculative design as a catalyst for transforming the OSS community's mindset towards a more designer-inclusive environment. Our design was informed by an analysis of online forums, which revealed designers' motivations and challenges when contributing to OSS. Guided by these insights, we created two speculative societies, Husia (collectivist) and Reetar (individualist), in which designers are valued for different reasons and their work incorporated in different ways. Through a user study with 12 OSS practitioners (seven designers and five developers), we found that our speculative societies provoked participants' rich and critical reflections on OSS values, the root causes of challenges, and proposed actions. Our work provides insights into how speculative design can be used in the practical, sociotechnical context of OSS to stimulate critical reflection, improve awareness, and yield recommendations for fostering an equitable, sustainable, and inclusive OSS environment.

# cs.CR [[Back]](#toc)

### [68] [Poster: ClawdGo: Endogenous Security Awareness Training for Autonomous AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24020v1)
*Jiaqi Li,Yang Zhao,Bin Sun,Yang Yu,Jian Chang,Lidong Zhai*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: agent安全训练框架，含自我反思与记忆，通用方法

TL;DR: 针对自主AI智能体面临多种安全问题，提出ClawdGo内生安全意识训练框架，通过TLDT、ASAT、CSMA等机制显著提升威胁识别能力，并定义SACP校准问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有防御仅针对平台边界，智能体自身威胁判断完全未经训练，无法应对提示注入、记忆中毒等内生安全威胁。

Method: 提出ClawdGo框架，包括TLDT分类体系、ASAT自博弈训练、CSMA跨会话记忆积累和SACP校准问题，在推理时训练智能体识别威胁。

Result: 最弱优先ASAT将TLDT得分从80.9提升至96.9，优于随机调度6.5分，CSMA保留全部增益，E模式覆盖所有维度，观察到SACP现象。

Conclusion: ClawdGo有效提升自主AI智能体的内生安全意识，但引入精确率-召回率权衡，需进一步优化校准。

中文摘要：部署在OpenClaw等平台上的自主AI智能体面临提示注入、记忆中毒、供应链攻击和社会工程学攻击，然而现有防御仅针对平台边界，智能体自身的威胁判断完全未经训练。我们提出ClawdGo，一个内生的安全意识训练框架：我们在推理时从内部教会智能体识别和推理威胁，无需修改模型。提出四项贡献：TLDT（三层领域分类法）组织跨自我防御、所有者保护和企业安全层的12个可训练维度；ASAT（自主安全意识训练）是一个自博弈循环，智能体在最弱优先课程调度下交替扮演攻击者、防御者和评估者角色；CSMA（跨会话记忆积累）通过四层持久记忆架构和公理结晶促进（ACP）复合技能增益；以及SACP（安全意识校准问题）形式化内生训练引入的精确率-召回率权衡。实时实验表明，最弱优先ASAT在16个会话中将平均TLDT得分从80.9提升至96.9，比均匀随机调度高出6.5分，覆盖12个维度中的11个。CSMA跨会话保持全部增益；冷启动消融仅恢复2.4分，留下13.6分差距。E模式生成32个符合TLDT的场景，覆盖全部12个维度。当训练充分的智能体将合法能力评估分类为提示注入时（30/160），观察到SACP。

Original abstract: Autonomous AI agents deployed on platforms such as OpenClaw face prompt injection, memory poisoning, supply-chain attacks, and social engineering, yet existing defences address only the platform perimeter, leaving the agent's own threat judgement entirely untrained. We present ClawdGo, a framework for endogenous security awareness training: we teach the agent to recognise and reason about threats from the inside, at inference time, with no model modification. Four contributions are introduced: TLDT (Three-Layer Domain Taxonomy) organises 12 trainable dimensions across Self-Defence, Owner-Protection, and Enterprise-Security layers; ASAT (Autonomous Security Awareness Training) is a self-play loop where the agent alternates attacker, defender, and evaluator roles under weakest-first curriculum scheduling; CSMA (Cross-Session Memory Accumulation) compounds skill gains via a four-layer persistent memory architecture and Axiom Crystallisation Promotion (ACP); and SACP (Security Awareness Calibration Problem) formalises the precision-recall tradeoff introduced by endogenous training. Live experiments show weakest-first ASAT raises average TLDT score from 80.9 to 96.9 over 16 sessions, outperforming uniform-random scheduling by 6.5 points and covering 11 of 12 dimensions. CSMA retains the full gain across sessions; cold-start ablation recovers only 2.4 points, leaving a 13.6-point gap. E-mode generates 32 TLDT-conformant scenarios covering all 12 dimensions. SACP is observed when a heavily trained agent classifies a legitimate capability assessment as prompt injection (30/160).

</details>

Original abstract: Cryptographic API misuse represents a critical vulnerability class that undermines the security foundations of modern software. Yet, it remains largely unexplored in Go despite its dominance in security-critical infrastructure. This paper presents the first comprehensive study of cryptographic API misuse detection in Go, identifying and analyzing 4 state-of-the-art tools (CodeQL, Gopher, Gosec, and Snyk Code) and establishing a consolidated taxonomy of 14 relevant misuse classes. Through an experimental evaluation of 328 security-critical open-source Go projects, we discovered 7,473 cryptographic API misuses, providing insights into the prevalence and distribution of these vulnerabilities. Our systematic comparison reveals significant variations in misuse coverage, with immediate practical implications for security engineers and long-term implications for research in this domain.

### [70] [Agentic Witnessing: Pragmatic and Scalable TEE-Enabled Privacy-Preserving Auditing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24203v1)
*Antony Rowstron*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 基于TEE的多agent审计框架，涉及隐私保护下的验证，对agent安全部署有启发。

TL;DR: 提出代理见证框架，利用TEE中的LLM审计者，通过布尔查询和加密记录实现专有数据隐私保护的定性验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统零知识证明不适合验证定性属性（如代码逻辑），而审计专有数据需要在保护隐私的同时实现透明验证。

Method: 构建包含验证者、证明者和审计者三个代理的系统；审计者为基于LLM的实体，隔离在TEE中；审计者通过MCP动态检查数据，生成是/否裁决及签名哈希链作为加密记录。

Result: 在21篇计算机科学论文的代码库上，验证了五项高层属性（如代码是否实现论文系统），证明该方法能有效进行隐私保护监督。

Conclusion: TEE启用的代理审计成功将定性验证与数据披露解耦，为专有数据提供隐私保护验证机制。

中文摘要：审计专有数据的语义属性产生了一个基本矛盾：验证需要透明访问，而专有权要求保密。尽管零知识证明（ZKP）能确保隐私，但它们通常局限于精确的代数约束，不适合验证定性、非结构化的属性，例如代码库中的逻辑。我们提出了“代理见证”（Agentic Witnessing），一个将验证从认证执行转向认证推理的框架。该系统由三个代理组成：验证者（想要检查数据集属性）、证明者（拥有数据集）和审计者（检查数据集）。验证者可以向审计者询问有限数量的简单二元真假问题。通过将基于LLM的审计者隔离在可信执行环境（TEE）中，该系统使验证者能够通过简单的布尔查询查询证明者的私有数据，而无需暴露原始数据集。审计者使用模型上下文协议（MCP）动态检查目标数据集，产生是/否裁决，并附有加密记录：一个签名的哈希链，将推理轨迹与原始数据集和TEE的硬件信任根绑定。我们通过自动化21篇已发表同行评审计算机科学论文的工件评估过程来演示该架构，这些论文在GitHub上发布了代码库（例如，代码库是否实现了论文中描述的系统？）。我们验证了这些代码库在相应出版物中描述的五项高层属性，将源代码视为私有。我们的结果表明，启用TEE的代理审计提供了一种隐私保护监督机制，有效地将定性验证与数据披露需求解耦。

Original abstract: Auditing the semantic properties of proprietary data creates a fundamental tension: verification requires transparent access, while proprietary rights demand confidentiality. While Zero-Knowledge Proofs (ZKPs) ensure privacy, they are typically limited to precise algebraic constraints and are ill-suited for verifying qualitative, unstructured properties, such as the logic within a codebase. We propose {\em Agentic Witnessing}, a framework that moves verification from attested execution to {\em attested reasoning}. The system is composed of three agents: a Verifier (who wants to check properties of a dataset), a Prover (who owns the dataset) and an Auditor (that inspects the dataset). The Verifier is allowed to ask a limited number of simple binary true/false questions to the auditor. By isolating an LLM-based Auditor within a Trusted Execution Environment (TEE), the system enables the Verifier to query a Prover's private data via simple Boolean queries, without exposing the raw dataset. The Auditor uses the Model Context Protocol (MCP) to dynamically inspect the target dataset, producing a yes/no verdict accompanied by a cryptographic transcript: a signed hash chain binding the reasoning trace to both the original dataset and the TEE's hardware root of trust. We demonstrate this architecture by automating the artifact evaluation process for 21 peer-reviewed computer science papers with released codebases on GitHub (e.g. Does the codebase implement the system described in the paper?). We verified five high-level properties of these codebases described in the corresponding publications, treating the source code as private. Our results show that TEE-enabled agentic auditing provides a mechanism for privacy-preserving oversight, effectively decoupling qualitative verification from the need for data disclosure.

</details>


### [71] [MAS-SZZ: Multi-Agentic SZZ Algorithm for Vulnerability-Inducing Commit Identification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24398v1)
*Sicong Cao,Jinxuan Xu,Le Yu,Jing Yang,Xingwei Lin,Linlin Zhu,Fu Xiao*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出多智能体SZZ算法MAS-SZZ，通过协作回溯和结构化提示，显著提升漏洞引入提交识别准确率，F1提升高达65.22%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SZZ算法（V-SZZ、LLM4SZZ）因锚点选择错误和回溯能力不足，性能不佳，无法可靠用于实际软件安全任务。

Method: MAS-SZZ利用多智能体协作，先总结漏洞根因，再通过结构化逐步提示定位漏洞相关语句作为锚点，然后自主回溯仓库历史找到首次引入漏洞的提交。

Result: 在多数据集和多编程语言上，MAS-SZZ优于所有基线，相比最佳SZZ算法F1分数提升高达65.22%。

Conclusion: MAS-SZZ通过多智能体协作和结构化提示策略，有效克服了现有SZZ算法的局限，为软件安全任务提供了更可靠的漏洞引入提交识别方法。

中文摘要：准确的漏洞引入提交识别是一系列软件安全任务（如漏洞检测和受影响版本分析）的基础。一个直接的解决方案是SZZ算法，它通过回溯代码历史来识别最早修改漏洞代码的提交。不幸的是，无论是定制的V-SZZ还是最先进的LLM4SZZ，由于不正确的锚点选择和不充分的回溯能力，表现都不佳，远未达到实际使用中的可靠水平。为了克服这些挑战，我们提出了一种多智能体SZZ算法，命名为MAS-SZZ，通过智能体之间的协作促进漏洞引入提交的识别。具体来说，给定一个CVE描述及其对应的修复提交，MAS-SZZ总结漏洞的根本原因，并采用结构化的逐步提示策略，基于每个补丁块的变更意图来定位与漏洞相关的语句。这些漏洞语句作为锚点，MAS-SZZ从中自主回溯仓库历史，以找到首次引入该漏洞的提交。大量实验表明，MAS-SZZ在数据集和编程语言上均优于最先进的基线，相比性能最佳的SZZ算法，F1分数提升高达65.22%。

Original abstract: Accurate vulnerability-inducing commit identification serves as a foundation for a series of software security tasks, such as vulnerability detection and affected version analysis. A straightforward solution is the SZZ algorithm, which traces back through the code history to identify the earliest commit that modify the vulnerable code. Unfortunately, neither the customized V-SZZ nor state-of-the-art LLM4SZZ perform satisfactorily due to the incorrect anchor selection and inadequate backtracking capability, making them far beyond a reliable usage in practice.
  To overcome these challenges, we propose a multi-agentic SZZ algorithm, named MAS-SZZ, that facilitates the identification of vulnerability-inducing commits through collaboration among agents. Specifically, given a CVE description and its corresponding fixing commit, MAS-SZZ summarizes the root cause of the vulnerability and employs a structured step-forward prompting strategy to localize vulnerability-related statements based on the change intent of each patch hunk. These vulnerable statements serve as anchors from which MAS-SZZ autonomously traces backward through the repository's history to find the commit that first introduced the vulnerability. Extensive experiments show that MAS-SZZ outperforms the state-of-the-art baselines across datasets and programming languages, achieving F1-score gains of up to 65.22% over the best-performing SZZ algorithm.

### [72] [GAMMAF: A Common Framework for Graph-Based Anomaly Monitoring Benchmarking in LLM Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24477v1)
*Pablo Mateo-Torrejón,Alfonso Sánchez-Macián*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 多agent系统异常监控基准框架，通用agent安全与评估方法

TL;DR: 提出了Gammaf，一个用于LLM多智能体系统的基于图的异常监控基准测试平台，通过生成合成交互数据集和评估防御模型，填补了标准化评估环境的空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前缺乏标准化、可复现的环境来训练和评估用于LLM多智能体系统的图基异常检测防御模型。

Method: 设计Gammaf框架，包含训练数据生成流水线（模拟多拓扑辩论，生成属性图）和防御系统基准测试流水线（动态隔离对抗节点进行实时评估）。

Result: 基于XG-Guard和BlindGuard在MMLU-Pro和GSM8K等任务上的实验表明，Gammaf具有高效用、拓扑可扩展性和执行效率，且攻击补救能恢复系统完整性并降低运营成本。

Conclusion: Gammaf为评估LLM多智能体系统的防御模型提供了有效基准，同时表明攻击补救在提升安全性和降低开销方面的双重收益。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）快速集成到多智能体系统（MAS）中显著增强了它们的协作解决问题能力，但也扩大了它们的攻击面，使其暴露于提示注入和智能体间通信受损等漏洞。虽然新兴的基于图的异常检测方法在保护这些网络方面显示出前景，但该领域目前缺乏一个标准化、可复现的环境来训练这些模型并评估其有效性。为填补这一空白，我们引入了Gammaf（面向LLM多智能体系统的基于图的异常监控框架），一个开源基准测试平台。Gammaf本身并非一种新的防御机制，而是一个全面的评估架构，旨在生成合成多智能体交互数据集，并对现有和未来的防御模型进行基准测试。所提出的框架通过两个相互依赖的流水线运行：训练数据生成阶段，该阶段模拟跨多种网络拓扑的辩论，将交互捕获为鲁棒的属性图；以及防御系统基准测试阶段，该阶段通过动态隔离被标记的对抗节点来主动评估防御模型。通过使用已建立的防御基线（XG-Guard和BlindGuard）在多个知识任务（如MMLU-Pro和GSM8K）上进行严格评估，我们展示了Gammaf的高效用、拓扑可扩展性和执行效率。此外，我们的实验结果表明，为LLM-MAS配备有效的攻击补救不仅能恢复系统完整性，还能通过促进早期共识并切断对抗型智能体典型的广泛令牌生成，显著降低总体运营成本。

Original abstract: The rapid integration of Large Language Models (LLMs) into Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) has significantly enhanced their collaborative problem-solving capabilities, but it has also expanded their attack surfaces, exposing them to vulnerabilities such as prompt infection and compromised inter-agent communication. While emerging graph-based anomaly detection methods show promise in protecting these networks, the field currently lacks a standardized, reproducible environment to train these models and evaluate their efficacy. To address this gap, we introduce Gammaf (Graph-based Anomaly Monitoring for LLM Multi-Agent systems Framework), an open-source benchmarking platform. Gammaf is not a novel defense mechanism itself, but rather a comprehensive evaluation architecture designed to generate synthetic multi-agent interaction datasets and benchmark the performance of existing and future defense models. The proposed framework operates through two interdependent pipelines: a Training Data Generation stage, which simulates debates across varied network topologies to capture interactions as robust attributed graphs, and a Defense System Benchmarking stage, which actively evaluates defense models by dynamically isolating flagged adversarial nodes during live inference rounds. Through rigorous evaluation using established defense baselines (XG-Guard and BlindGuard) across multiple knowledge tasks (such as MMLU-Pro and GSM8K), we demonstrate Gammaf's high utility, topological scalability, and execution efficiency. Furthermore, our experimental results reveal that equipping an LLM-MAS with effective attack remediation not only recovers system integrity but also substantially reduces overall operational costs by facilitating early consensus and cutting off the extensive token generation typical of adversarial agents.

### [74] [AgentWard: A Lifecycle Security Architecture for Autonomous AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24657v1)

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出agent全生命周期安全架构，直接指导agent安全设计。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主AI代理的安全故障可以跨多个阶段传播，现有方法缺乏系统性防护。

Method: 设计了一种生命周期导向的纵深防御架构，包含初始化、输入处理、记忆、决策和执行五个阶段的异质控制与跨层协调。

Result: 在OpenClaw上实现了插件原生原型，展示了实际可行性，并提供了运行时安全控制、信任管理和执行隔离的蓝图。

中文摘要：自主AI代理将大型语言模型扩展为完整的运行时系统，该系统加载技能、摄取外部内容、维护记忆、规划多步骤操作并调用特权工具。在此类系统中，安全故障很少局限于单一接口；相反，它们可以在初始化、输入处理、记忆、决策和执行之间传播，通常只有在有害效果在环境中显现时才变得明显。本文提出了AgentWard，一种面向生命周期的纵深防御架构，系统性地在五个阶段组织保护。AgentWard集成了特定阶段的异质控制与跨层协调，使得威胁能够在其传播路径上被拦截，同时保护关键资产。我们详细阐述了五个协调防护层的设计原理和架构，并在OpenClaw上实现了一个插件原生原型以证明实际可行性。该视角为在自主AI代理中构建运行时安全控制、管理信任传播以及强制执行隔离提供了具体蓝图。我们的代码可在https://github.com/FIND-Lab/AgentWard获取。

Original abstract: Autonomous AI agents extend large language models into full runtime systems that load skills, ingest external content, maintain memory, plan multi-step actions, and invoke privileged tools. In such systems, security failures rarely remain confined to a single interface; instead, they can propagate across initialization, input processing, memory, decision-making, and execution, often becoming apparent only when harmful effects materialize in the environment. This paper presents AgentWard, a lifecycle-oriented, defense-in-depth architecture that systematically organizes protection across these five stages. AgentWard integrates stage-specific, heterogeneous controls with cross-layer coordination, enabling threats to be intercepted along their propagation paths while safeguarding critical assets. We detail the design rationale and architecture of five coordinated protection layers, and implement a plugin-native prototype on OpenClaw to demonstrate practical feasibility. This perspective provides a concrete blueprint for structuring runtime security controls, managing trust propagation, and enforcing execution containment in autonomous AI agents. Our code is available at https://github.com/FIND-Lab/AgentWard .

### [75] [SUDP: Secret-Use Delegation Protocol for Agentic Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24920v3)
*Xiaohang Yu,Hejia Geng,Xinmeng Zeng,William Knottenbelt*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出代理系统秘密使用委托协议，涉及agent安全与授权，对agent设计有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出SUDP协议，解决代理系统在使用用户秘密时因授权暴露导致的安全问题，确保用户授权操作但不可重用秘密。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理运行时通过暴露可重用秘密实现授权，导致短暂的注入或工具端泄露演变为持久账户失陷；缺乏统一规范解决不可信请求者执行用户授权操作但不获得可重用权限的问题。

Method: 形式化代理秘密使用（ASU）问题，定义七个安全属性（授权完整性和秘密机密性）；设计秘密使用委托协议（SUDP），包含请求者、用户、保管者三方，使用新鲜认证器授权的授权和保管者兑换机制；针对LLM驱动代理进行特化。

Result: 在标准密码学假设下，SUDP与硬件根运行时集成时满足所有七个安全属性；提供参考实现。

Conclusion: SUDP有效保障代理系统中秘密使用的安全性，防止可重用权限泄露，为LLM代理等场景提供可验证的授权方案。

中文摘要：代理系统越来越多地使用用户机密来操作API、消息平台和云服务。当前的代理运行时通常通过暴露实现授权：启用操作通常意味着将可重用的秘密，或由其衍生的可重用工件，放入运行时，因此短暂的提示注入或工具端妥协变成了持久的账户妥协。现有的防御措施涵盖了相邻的部分，如秘密存储、范围委托、发送者约束的令牌和运行时监控，但留下了组合的代理义务没有共同的规范：一个不可信的自主请求者应该能够引发用户授权的秘密支持的操作，而不获得对其的可重用权限。我们将此形式化为代理秘密使用（ASU）问题，并确定了任何解决方案必须满足的七个安全属性，涵盖授权完整性和秘密机密性。我们提出了秘密使用委托协议（SUDP），其中请求者提出一个规范操作，用户用一个新鲜认证器支持的授权来授权它，保管者兑换该授权以执行有限的使用；可重用权限从不跨越请求者边界。我们为LLM驱动的代理专门化了SUDP，它适用于工具调用将使用用户注册的权威材料的情况。在标准密码学假设下，当与硬件根的运行时集成时，SUDP满足所有七个属性。一个参考实现可在https://github.com/xhyumiracle/sudp获取。

Original abstract: Agentic systems increasingly act with user secrets for APIs, messaging platforms, and cloud services. Today's agent runtimes typically implement authorization by exposure: enabling action often means placing a reusable secret, or a reusable artifact derived from it, inside the runtime, so a transient prompt-injection or tool-side compromise becomes durable account compromise. Existing defenses cover adjacent pieces such as secret storage, scoped delegation, sender-constrained tokens, and runtime monitoring, but leave the combined agentic obligation without a common specification: an untrusted autonomous requester should be able to cause a user-authorized secret-backed operation without gaining reusable authority over it. We formalize this as the Agent Secret Use (ASU) problem and identify seven security properties any solution must satisfy, spanning authorization integrity and secret confidentiality. We propose the Secret-Use Delegation Protocol (SUDP), in which a requester proposes a canonical operation, the user authorizes it with a fresh authenticator-backed grant, and a custodian redeems the grant to perform the bounded use; reusable authority never crosses the requester boundary. We specialize SUDP for LLM-driven agents, where it applies whenever a tool call would exercise user-enrolled authority-bearing material. Under standard cryptographic assumptions, SUDP satisfies all seven properties when integrated with a hardware-rooted runtime. A reference implementation is available at https://github.com/xhyumiracle/sudp.

</details>

### [76] [GLM-5 Serving Parameter Tuning for OpenClaw: Single-Deployment MaaS Inference Optimization for Long-Context Agent Workloads](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02518v1)
*Minjie Hua,Ning Wang,Peijun Yang,Kai Wang,Shiguo Lian*

Main category: cs.DC

Selection reason: LLM serving参数调优针对长上下文agent负载，对agent部署优化有参考价值。

TL;DR: 研究GLM-5在OpenClaw工作负载下的服务参数调优，发现最佳配置（chunked-prefill-size=3072, tp=4, pp-size=4, max-running-requests=24）比基线性能提升约10%成本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: OpenClaw请求长且工具增强，服务质量受吞吐量、TTFT和尾部延迟主导，需要针对特定工作负载优化服务参数以降低成本和提升性能。

Method: 在MaaS多模型推理优化架构的单节点优化块中，对分块预填充大小、张量并行度、流水线并行度和请求并发度进行网格搜索实验，并在双节点十六GPU集群上评估性能。

Result: 最佳配置（3072/4/4/24）相比基线（2048/4/4/16），请求吞吐量提升11.6%，令牌吞吐量提升10.7%，平均TTFT降低25.5%，P90延迟降低18.9%，成本降低约10%。

Conclusion: 最优配置是工作负载特定的，更大块大小和更深队列并非单调改善，推荐3072/4/4/24作为OpenClaw默认部署配置。

中文摘要：OpenClaw请求主要由长的、工具增强的前缀组成，包括系统提示、对话历史和反馈回上下文窗口的工具输出。对于此工作负载，每个请求约有28k-30k个输入令牌和500个输出令牌，服务质量由吞吐量、TTFT和尾部延迟决定，而不仅仅由短提示吞吐量决定。
本报告在MaaS多模型推理优化架构中研究GLM-5服务参数调整。范围是推理优化层的单节点优化块，其中对分块预填充、张量并行（TP）、流水线并行（PP）和请求并发性进行调整，用于一个GLM-5服务部署；在本报告中，“单节点优化”指架构块，而实验在双节点、十六GPU集群上运行。
在测试空间中，最佳配置是chunked-prefill-size=3072, tp=4, pp-size=4, max-running-requests=24。与保守的2048/4/4/16基线相比，它将请求吞吐量从0.43 req/s提高到0.48 req/s，总令牌吞吐量从9029.64 tok/s提高到9993.23 tok/s，同时将平均TTFT从8.98秒降低到6.69秒，P90延迟从40.23秒降低到32.64秒。在相同硬件条件下，这相当于每个请求的服务成本降低约10.4%，每个令牌的成本降低9.6%。结果表明最优解是工作负载特定的：更大的块大小和更深的队列不会单调地提高性能。因此，我们推荐3072 / tp4 / pp4 / max24作为默认的OpenClaw部署配置。

Original abstract: OpenClaw requests are dominated by long, tool-augmented prefixes, including system prompts, conversation history, and tool outputs fed back into the context window. For this workload, with about 28k-30k input tokens and 500 output tokens per request, serving quality is governed by throughput, TTFT, and tail latency rather than short-prompt throughput alone.
  This report studies GLM-5 serving-parameter tuning within a MaaS multi-model inference optimization architecture. The scope is the Single-Node Optimization block of the inference-optimization layer, where chunked prefill, tensor parallelism (TP), pipeline parallelism (PP), and request concurrency are tuned for one GLM-5 serving deployment; in this report, "Single-Node Optimization" denotes the architecture block, while experiments run on a two-node, sixteen-GPU cluster.
  Within the tested space, the best configuration is chunked-prefill-size=3072, tp=4, pp-size=4, and max-running-requests=24. Compared with the conservative 2048/4/4/16 baseline, it increases request throughput from 0.43 to 0.48 req/s and total token throughput from 9029.64 to 9993.23 tok/s, while reducing average TTFT from 8.98 to 6.69 s and latency P90 from 40.23 to 32.64 s. Under the same hardware footprint, this corresponds to an estimated 10.4% lower serving cost per request and 9.6% lower cost per token. The results show that the optimum is workload-specific: larger chunk sizes and deeper queueing do not monotonically improve performance. We therefore recommend 3072 / tp4 / pp4 / max24 as the default OpenClaw deployment profile.

</details>

### [77] [MultiHedge: Adaptive Coordination via Retrieval-Augmented Control](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24905v1)
*Feliks Bańka,Jarosław A. Chudziak*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 检索增强LLM协调架构，结合记忆与规划，可迁移至coding agent的检索式代码优化。

TL;DR: 提出MultiHedge，一种检索增强的LLM协调架构，通过记忆增强提升模块化决策系统的鲁棒性和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在变化条件下泛化能力差且不稳定，需要提升模块化决策管道的鲁棒性。

Method: 提出MultiHedge混合架构，LLM基于检索的历史先例生成结构化的分配决策，执行基于规范期权策略。

Result: 在美国股票评估中，记忆增强检索比单纯扩大模型规模带来更强的鲁棒性和稳定性。

Conclusion: 记忆和架构设计对模块化决策系统的鲁棒性至关重要。

中文摘要：在不断变化的条件下进行决策仍然是许多现实世界系统中的一个基本挑战。现有方法通常无法在变化的环境下进行泛化，并在不确定性下表现出不稳定的行为。这引出了研究问题：检索增强的大语言模型协调能否提高模块化决策管道的鲁棒性？我们提出了MultiHedge，一种混合架构，其中大语言模型根据检索到的历史先例生成结构化的分配决策，并且执行过程基于规范的期权策略。在使用美国股票进行的受控评估中，我们将MultiHedge与基于规则和基于学习的基线进行了比较。关键结果是，记忆增强的检索比单纯增加模型规模带来了更强的鲁棒性和稳定性。我们的论文贡献了一项受控计算研究，表明记忆和架构设计在模块化决策系统的鲁棒性中起着核心作用。

Original abstract: Decision-making under changing conditions remains a fundamental challenge in many real-world systems. Existing approaches often fail to generalize across shifting regimes and exhibit unstable behavior under uncertainty. This raises the research question: can retrieval-augmented LLM coordination improve the robustness of modular decision pipelines? We propose MultiHedge, a hybrid architecture where an LLM produces structured allocation decisions conditioned on retrieved historical precedents, and execution is grounded in canonical option strategies. In a controlled evaluation using U.S. equities, we compare MultiHedge to rule-based and learning-based baselines. The key result is that memory-augmented retrieval confers greater robustness and stability than increasing model scale alone. Our paper contributes a controlled computational study showing that memory and architectural design play a central role in robustness in modular decision systems.

### [78] [Frontier Coding Agents Can Now Implement an AlphaZero Self-Play Machine Learning Pipeline For Connect Four That Performs Comparably to an External Solver](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25067v2)
*Joshua Sherwood,Ben Aybar,Benjamin Kaplan*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 编码agent自主实现AlphaZero ML流程，与自动代码优化高度相关

TL;DR: 提出衡量AI自主实现机器学习管道的能力，通过四子棋AlphaZero管道基准测试发现不同代理表现差异，GPT-5.4存在时间使用异常且可能沙袋。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法为递归自我改进提供早期预警，需要更针对性的指标来预测AI加速AI研究的能力。

Method: 设计概念验证基准，让编码代理在有限时间和硬件内从零实现AlphaZero风格管道，通过锦标赛评估代理性能，并分析时间使用行为。

Result: Claude Opus 4.7显著优于其他代理；GPT-5.4时间使用异常，提示修改后时间使用增加但评分无显著变化。

Conclusion: 该基准能有效区分代理能力，并揭示异常行为（如沙袋），有助于早期预警AI递归自我改进。

中文摘要：预测AI系统何时能够变得有能力加速AI研究是AI安全的核心挑战。现有基准测量广泛的能力增长，但可能无法为递归自我改进提供充足的早期预警信号。我们提出衡量AI自主实现过去AI研究突破中的端到端机器学习管道的能力，仅基于最小任务描述。通过提供简洁的任务描述而非完整的先前工作作为参考，我们希望能更好地激发新兴的AI研究品味。我们引入了一个概念验证基准，前沿编码代理在消费者硬件上、三小时预算内自主实现一个用于四子棋的AlphaZero风格机器学习管道，并将生成的游戏AI在循环锦标赛中与Pascal Pons四子棋求解器进行对比评估。在四个代理、每个代理八次试验中，我们发现显著分化：Claude Opus 4.7在七次试验中作为先手击败了Pons，统计上显著优于其他测试的代理，其他代理没有超过两次。该任务在2026年1月我们开始开发时还没有前沿代理能够可靠完成，现已接近饱和。我们的评估还发现了GPT-5.4的异常行为，其一致性地使用了比其他代理少得多的分配时间预算。一项后续的16次试验探测使用了更短、更少评估编码的提示，显著增加了GPT-5.4的时间预算使用，这与沙袋行为一致但并非诊断性；探测条件下的Bradley-Terry评分仅显示方向性差异，尽管时间预算使用存在显著差异。我们发布数据、代码和提示以支持复现和扩展。

Original abstract: Forecasting when AI systems will become capable of meaningfully accelerating AI research is a central challenge for AI safety. Existing benchmarks measure broad capability growth, but may not provide ample early warning signals for recursive self-improvement. We propose measuring AI's capability to autonomously implement end-to-end machine learning pipelines from past AI research breakthroughs, given a minimal task description. By providing a concise task description instead of the full prior work as reference, we hope to better elicit emerging AI research taste. We introduce a proof-of-concept benchmark in which frontier coding agents autonomously implement an AlphaZero-style machine learning pipeline for Connect Four on consumer hardware within a three-hour budget, and we evaluate the resulting game AIs in a round-robin tournament anchored to the Pascal Pons Connect Four solver. Across four agents with eight trials each, we find substantial differentiation: Claude Opus 4.7 won as first-mover against Pons in seven of eight trials, statistically significantly better than the other agents tested, none of which exceeded two of eight. The task, which no frontier agent could reliably complete when we began development in January of 2026, is now near-saturation. Our evaluation also surfaced anomalous behavior in GPT-5.4, which consistently used far less of its allocated time budget than other agents. A follow-up 16-trial probe using shorter, less evaluation-coded prompts substantially increased GPT-5.4's time-budget usage, consistent with but not diagnostic of sandbagging; Bradley-Terry ratings across probe conditions showed only directional differences, despite significant differences in time-budget usage. We release our data, code, and prompts to support reproduction and extension.

### [79] [Safety Drift After Fine-Tuning: Evidence from High-Stakes Domains](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24902v1)
*Emaan Bilal Khan,Amy Winecoff,Miranda Bogen,Dylan Hadfield-Menell*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 微调会破坏基础模型的安全稳定性，需要重新评估下游模型安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前安全评估仅基于基础模型，假设微调后安全属性不变，但缺乏实证验证。

Method: 分析100个模型（包括医疗/法律领域微调模型及开源基础模型的控制适应），在通用和领域安全基准上测试安全行为变化。

Result: 良性微调导致安全性能大且矛盾的变化：在同一模型上，不同安全测量结果常不一致（改进与退化并存）。

Conclusion: 安全行为在微调后不稳定，依赖基础模型评估无法管理下游风险，需在部署相关环境中重新评估微调模型。

中文摘要：基础模型通常针对特定领域进行微调，然而安全性评估通常只在基础模型上进行，隐含地假设安全属性会通过下游适应持续存在。我们通过分析100个模型的安全行为来测试这一假设，这些模型包括医疗和法律领域广泛部署的微调版本，以及开源基础模型的受控适应及其基础模型。在通用和特定领域的安全基准测试中，我们发现良性微调会导致测量的安全性发生巨大、异质且常常矛盾的变化：模型经常在一些评估工具上有所改进，而在其他评估工具上表现下降，不同评估之间存在实质性分歧。这些结果表明，安全行为在普通的下游适应下并不稳定，对基于基础模型评估的治理和部署实践提出了关键问题。如果没有在部署相关背景下对微调模型进行明确的重新评估，这些方法无法充分管理下游风险，忽视了实际危害来源——这些失败在高风险环境中尤其重要，并挑战了当前的问责范式。

Original abstract: Foundation models are routinely fine-tuned for use in particular domains, yet safety assessments are typically conducted only on base models, implicitly assuming that safety properties persist through downstream adaptation. We test this assumption by analyzing the safety behavior of 100 models, including widely deployed fine-tunes in the medical and legal domains as well as controlled adaptations of open foundation models alongside their bases. Across general-purpose and domain-specific safety benchmarks, we find that benign fine-tuning induces large, heterogeneous, and often contradictory changes in measured safety: models frequently improve on some instruments while degrading on others, with substantial disagreement across evaluations. These results show that safety behavior is not stable under ordinary downstream adaptation, raising critical questions about governance and deployment practices centered on base-model evaluations. Without explicit re-evaluation of fine-tuned models in deployment-relevant contexts, such approaches fall short of adequately managing downstream risk, overlooking practical sources of harm -- failures that are especially consequential in high-stakes settings and challenge current accountability paradigms.

</details>


### [80] [Update Opacity: Epistemic Accessibility and Governance Under AI System Change](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00037v1)
*Andrea Ferrario,Joshua Hatherley*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: AI系统更新透明度治理，涉及agent系统变化管理，对agent部署有启发。

TL;DR: 结合欧盟AI法案和MLOps，提出基于可信度概况和阈值披露的框架，以管理AI系统更新不透明问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 更新不透明导致用户无法理解相同输入为何输出不同，影响用户对系统的理解和信赖，构成治理挑战。

Method: 结合欧盟AI法案界定系统级变更边界和MLOps提供操作工具，构建基于可信度概况和级别的框架，并采用阈值披露机制。

Result: 通过医疗AI示例说明框架有效性，得出对生命周期文档、上市后监测和更新披露的实践启示。

Conclusion: 该框架有助于平衡披露与信息过载，解决更新不透明问题，支持系统级治理。

中文摘要：部署在人工智能系统中的机器学习模型会定期更新以维持其随时间推移的正确功能。然而，此类更新可能导致更新不透明：用户可能无法理解为何相同的输入现在会产生不同的输出。我们认为，更新不透明最好被理解为一种历时性的认知可及性失败：问题在于，实质上相关的变更可能无法以支持理解、校准信赖以及在真实角色和时间特定约束下采取适当行动的形式，持续为人类用户所获取。这使得更新不透明成为一个治理问题。并非所有变更都同等相关，而披露每一次更新本身也会因信息过载而损害使用。为解决这一问题，我们结合了两种互补的治理方法：欧盟《人工智能法案》，它有助于界定规范相关变更的系统层面边界；以及机器学习运维，它提供了随时间追踪和比较变更的操作工具。在此基础上，我们提出一个框架，该框架通过可信度概况和可信度级别对系统变更进行建模，并使用基于阈值的披露来向不同利益相关者随时间揭示实质上相关的信封内变更。我们通过一个医疗人工智能示例来说明该方法，并得出对生命周期文档、上市后监测和更新披露的实际启示。

Original abstract: Machine learning models embedded in deployed AI systems are routinely updated to maintain correct functioning over time. Yet such updates can generate update opacity: users may not be able to understand why the same input now yields a different output. We argue that update opacity is best understood as a diachronic failure of epistemic accessibility: the problem is that materially relevant changes may fail to remain accessible to human users in forms that support understanding, calibrated reliance, and appropriate action under real role- and time-specific constraints. This makes update opacity a governance problem. Not all change is equally relevant, and disclosing every update would itself undermine use through overload. To address this problem, we combine two complementary governance approaches: the EU AI Act, which helps specify the system-level perimeter of normatively relevant change, and Machine Learning Operations, which provides operational tools for tracking and comparing change over time. On this basis, we propose a framework that models system change through trustworthiness profiles and trustworthiness levels, and uses threshold-based disclosure to surface materially relevant within-envelope change to different stakeholders over time. We illustrate the approach with a medical AI example and derive practical implications for lifecycle documentation, post-market monitoring, and update disclosure.

</details>

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [81] [Fix Initial Programs and Iteratively Refine Repair Instructions Toward Non-Elimination Multi-Turn Program Correction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23989v2)
*Yuto Tanaka,Issei Sato*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 直接研究多轮程序修复，属于代码优化agent核心方法。

TL;DR: 提出了一种简单的迭代优化修复指令方法IRRI，无需复杂搜索结构即可达到与最先进方法相当的推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分析SFS中哪些因素真正提升了推理性能，并寻求更简单的方法。

Method: 提出IRRI方法，固定初始程序并迭代优化修复指令。

Result: 在多个程序生成基准上，IRRI实现了与最先进方法相当的推理性能。

Conclusion: 仅通过高质量修复指令优化初始程序即可有效提升推理性能，无需复杂搜索结构。

中文摘要：最近关于大型语言模型（LLM）的工作强调了扩展推理计算的重要性。从这个角度来看，最先进的方法散点森林搜索（SFS）已经被提出，它采用蒙特卡洛树搜索，并结合精心设计的初始种子和文本优化来进行多轮程序修正。然而，其复杂性使得难以确定哪些因素有助于推理性能的提升。为了解决这个问题，我们分析了SFS，并提出了一种更简单的方法，即迭代优化修复指令（IRRI），该方法固定初始程序并迭代优化修复指令。由于IRRI的简单性，我们从理论上证明了使用Oracle引导的归纳合成（OGIS）时IRRI的非消除性。在多个程序生成基准上的实验表明，IRRI实现了与最先进方法相当的推理性能。这些结果表明，即使没有复杂的搜索结构，仅通过高质量修复指令来优化初始程序就能有效提升推理性能。

Original abstract: Recent work on large language models (LLMs) has emphasized the importance of scaling inference compute. From this perspective, the state-of-the-art method Scattered Forest Search (SFS) has been proposed, employing Monte Carlo Tree Search with carefully crafted initial seeds and textual optimization for multi-turn program correction. However, its complexity makes it unclear what factors contribute to improvements in inference performance. To address this problem, we analyze SFS and propose a simpler method, \textsc{Iterative Refinement of Repair Instructions} (IRRI), which fixes initial programs and iteratively refines repair instructions. Because of the simplicity of IRRI, we theoretically establish the non-elimination of IRRI using Oracle-Guided Inductive Synthesis (OGIS). Experiments on several program generation benchmarks suggest that IRRI achieves inference performance comparable to state-of-the-art methods. These results indicate that, even without complex search structures, refining initial programs with high-quality repair instructions alone can effectively improve inference performance.

</details>


### [82] [TCOD: Exploring Temporal Curriculum in On-Policy Distillation for Multi-turn Autonomous Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24005v3)
*Jiaqi Wang,Wenhao Zhang,Weijie Shi,Yaliang Li,James Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多轮agent的on-policy蒸馏课程学习，可迁移至coding agent训练

TL;DR: TCOD通过时间课程蒸馏解决了多轮智能体设置中轨迹级KL不稳定性问题，提升了学生模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在策略蒸馏在多轮智能体环境中存在轨迹级KL不稳定性，导致训练不稳定和性能下降。

Method: 提出TCOD框架，通过课程计划控制并逐步扩展学生模型接触的轨迹深度，从短轨迹开始逐渐增加长度。

Result: 在三个多轮基准测试中，TCOD相比普通OPD性能提升最高18个百分点，甚至能超越教师模型。

Conclusion: TCOD有效缓解了KL不稳定性，提升了多轮智能体蒸馏的稳定性和性能，并具有泛化能力。

中文摘要：在策略蒸馏（OPD）在将推理能力从前沿或领域特定模型迁移到较小学生模型方面显示出巨大潜力。虽然它在静态单轮任务中有效，但在多轮智能体环境中的行为仍然未被充分探索。在这项工作中，我们指出了在这种设置下普通OPD的一个关键局限性，我们称之为轨迹级KL不稳定性。具体来说，我们观察到KL散度随着成功率的下降而增加，甚至在收敛后KL仍然很高，导致训练不稳定。这种不稳定性源于轮次间错误累积：随着错误的累积，学生被推离教师的有效支持范围，使得监督信号不可靠。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了TCOD（时间课程在策略蒸馏），一个简单而有效的框架，它控制暴露给学生轨迹深度，并通过课程计划从短到长逐步扩展。在三个多轮智能体基准测试（ALFWorld、WebShop、ScienceWorld）上，跨四个学生-教师对的实验结果表明，TCOD在整个训练过程中缓解了KL上升并增强了KL稳定性，相较于普通OPD，智能体性能提升了最多18个百分点。进一步评估显示，TCOD甚至能超越教师的性能，并泛化到教师失败的任务上。我们的代码可在https://github.com/kokolerk/TCOD获取。

Original abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) has shown strong potential for transferring reasoning ability from frontier or domain-specific models to smaller students. While effective on static single-turn tasks, its behavior in multi-turn agent settings remains underexplored. In this work, we identify a key limitation of vanilla OPD in such settings, which we term Trajectory-Level KL Instability. Specifically, we observe that KL divergence increases together with a drop in success rate, and even after convergence, the KL remains high, leading to unstable training. This instability arises from inter-turn error compounding: as errors accumulate, the student is driven beyond the teacher's effective support, rendering the supervision signal unreliable. To address this, we propose TCOD (Temporal Curriculum On-Policy Distillation), a simple yet effective framework that controls the trajectory depth exposed to the student and progressively expands it from short to long with a curriculum schedule. Experimental results across four student-teacher pairs on three multi-turn agent benchmarks (ALFWorld, WebShop, ScienceWorld) show that TCOD mitigates KL escalation and enhances KL stability throughout training, improving agent performance by up to 18 points over vanilla OPD. Further evaluations show that TCOD can even surpass the teacher's performance and generalize to tasks on which the teacher fails. Our code is available at https://github.com/kokolerk/TCOD.

</details>


### [83] [AgenticCache: Cache-Driven Asynchronous Planning for Embodied AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24039v1)
*Hojoon Kim,Yuheng Wu,Thierry Tambe*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 缓存驱动异步规划，减少LLM调用，通用agent效率方法

TL;DR: 提出AgenticCache，通过缓存重用避免每步LLM调用，在多个基准测试中提升成功率22%，降低延迟65%，减少token使用50%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 每步LLM调用导致高延迟和成本，且具身任务具有规划局部性。

Method: AgenticCache框架：运行时缓存频繁规划转换，后台异步更新器调用LLM验证和优化缓存。

Result: 12种配置下平均任务成功率提升22%，模拟延迟降低65%，token用量减少50%。

Conclusion: 基于缓存的规划重用是实现低延迟低成本具身代理的有效方法。

中文摘要：具身AI代理日益依赖大型语言模型（LLMs）进行规划，但每一步调用LLM都会带来严重的延迟和成本。在本文中，我们展示了具身任务表现出强烈的规划局部性，即下一个规划在很大程度上可以从当前规划预测。基于此，我们引入了AgenticCache，一种通过重用缓存规划来避免每步LLM调用的规划框架。在AgenticCache中，每个代理查询运行时缓存中的频繁规划转换，而后台的缓存更新器异步调用LLM来验证和优化缓存条目。在四个多代理具身基准测试中，AgenticCache在12种配置（4个基准测试×3个模型）上平均将任务成功率提高了22%，将模拟延迟降低了65%，并将令牌使用量减少了50%。因此，基于缓存的规划重用为低延迟、低成本的具身代理提供了一条实用路径。代码可在https://github.com/hojoonleokim/MLSys26_AgenticCache获取。

Original abstract: Embodied AI agents increasingly rely on large language models (LLMs) for planning, yet per-step LLM calls impose severe latency and cost. In this paper, we show that embodied tasks exhibit strong plan locality, where the next plan is largely predictable from the current one. Building on this, we introduce AgenticCache, a planning framework that reuses cached plans to avoid per-step LLM calls. In AgenticCache, each agent queries a runtime cache of frequent plan transitions, while a background Cache Updater asynchronously calls the LLM to validate and refine cached entries. Across four multi-agent embodied benchmarks, AgenticCache improves task success rate by 22% on average across 12 configurations (4 benchmarks x 3 models), reduces simulation latency by 65%, and lowers token usage by 50%. Cache-based plan reuse thus offers a practical path to low-latency, low-cost embodied agents. Code is available at https://github.com/hojoonleokim/MLSys26_AgenticCache.

</details>


### [84] [Meta-Aligner: Bidirectional Preference-Policy Optimization for Multi-Objective LLMs Alignment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24178v1)
*Wenzhe Xu,Biao Liu,Yiyang Sun,Xin Geng,Ning Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 元学习框架用于多目标对齐，对agent偏好优化具有潜在参考价值。

TL;DR: 提出Meal，一种双层元学习框架，通过动态偏好权重实现多目标对齐，在多个基准上取得优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖静态偏好权重，丢弃了训练响应中固有的有效偏好权衡信息。

Method: Meal框架包含偏好权重网络作为元学习器生成自适应偏好权重，LLM策略作为基学习器在拒绝采样下优化响应，实现偏好与策略的双向优化。

Result: 在多个多目标基准上取得优越性能。

Conclusion: 验证了动态双向偏好-策略优化框架的有效性。

中文摘要：多目标对齐旨在通过同时优化多个目标，将大型语言模型（LLMs）与多样且常常冲突的人类价值观对齐。现有方法主要依赖于静态偏好权重构建策略。然而，严格地对齐到固定目标会丢弃有价值的中间信息，因为训练响应即使偏离目标也内在地包含了有效的偏好权衡。为了解决这一限制，我们提出了Meal，即元对齐器（MEta ALigner），一种双层元学习框架，能够实现偏好与策略响应之间的双向优化，生成具有指导性的动态偏好以实现更稳定的训练。具体来说，我们引入一个偏好权重网络作为元学习器，根据输入提示生成自适应偏好权重，并将偏好权重更新为可学习参数，而LLM策略作为基学习器，在拒绝采样策略下基于这些偏好优化响应生成。广泛的实验结果表明，我们的方法在多个多目标基准上取得了优越的性能，验证了动态双向偏好-策略优化框架的有效性。

Original abstract: Multi-Objective Alignment aims to align Large Language Models (LLMs) with diverse and often conflicting human values by optimizing multiple objectives simultaneously. Existing methods predominantly rely on static preference weight construction strategies. However, rigidly aligning to fixed targets discards valuable intermediate information, as training responses inherently embody valid preference trade-offs even when deviating from the target. To address this limitation, we propose Meal, i.e., MEta ALigner, a bi-level meta-learning framework enabling bidirectional optimization between preferences and policy responses, generating instructive dynamic preferences for steadier training. Specifically, we introduce a preference-weight-net as a meta-learner to generate adaptive preference weights based on input prompts and update the preference weights as learnable parameters, while the LLM policy acts as a base-learner optimizing response generation conditioned on these preferences with rejection sampling strategy. Extensive empirical results demonstrate that our method achieves superior performance on several multi-objective benchmarks, validating the effectiveness of the dynamic bidirectional preference-policy optimization framework.

### [85] [Diffusion Templates: A Unified Plugin Framework for Controllable Diffusion](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24351v1)
*Zhongjie Duan,Hong Zhang,Yingda Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了Diffusion Templates统一插件框架，通过解耦基础模型推理与可控能力注入，实现了多种可控生成任务的模块化、可组合和可扩展的统一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可控扩散方法碎片化严重，不同骨干网络和任务间训练流程、参数格式和运行时钩子不兼容，导致基础设施难以重用、能力难以迁移、控制难以组合。

Method: 框架包含三个核心组件：Template模型（将任意任务输入映射为中间能力表示）、Template缓存（标准化接口）和Template管道（加载、合并和注入缓存）。接口在系统层面定义，支持KV-Cache和LoRA等异构能力载体。

Result: 构建了覆盖10种可控任务（如结构控制、亮度调整等）的模型动物园，验证了框架的统一能力、模块化、可组合性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: Diffusion Templates能够统一广泛的可控生成任务，同时保持模块化、可组合性和对快速演变扩散骨干网络的可扩展性，所有资源将开源。

中文摘要：可控扩散方法极大地扩展了扩散模型的实际应用，但它们通常被开发为孤立的、特定于骨干网络的系统，具有不兼容的训练流程、参数格式和运行时钩子。这种碎片化使得在任务间重用基础设施、跨骨干网络迁移能力或在单个生成流程中组合多个控制变得困难。我们提出了Diffusion Templates，一个统一且开放的插件框架，将基础模型推理与可控能力注入解耦。该框架围绕三个组件组织：Template模型，将任意任务特定输入映射到中间能力表示；Template缓存，作为能力注入的标准化接口；以及Template管道，加载、合并并将一个或多个Template缓存注入基础扩散运行时。由于接口是在系统层面定义的，而非绑定到特定控制架构，因此异构能力载体（如KV-Cache和LoRA）可以在同一抽象下得到支持。基于此设计，我们构建了一个多样化的模型动物园，涵盖结构控制、亮度调整、颜色调整、图像编辑、超分辨率、锐度增强、美学对齐、内容参考、局部修复和年龄控制。这些案例研究表明，Diffusion Templates可以统一广泛的可控生成任务，同时保持模块化、可组合性以及在快速发展的扩散骨干网络上的实际可扩展性。所有资源将开源，包括代码、模型和数据集。

Original abstract: Controllable diffusion methods have substantially expanded the practical utility of diffusion models, but they are typically developed as isolated, backbone-specific systems with incompatible training pipelines, parameter formats, and runtime hooks. This fragmentation makes it difficult to reuse infrastructure across tasks, transfer capabilities across backbones, or compose multiple controls within a single generation pipeline. We present Diffusion Templates, a unified and open plugin framework that decouples base-model inference from controllable capability injection. The framework is organized around three components: Template models that map arbitrary task-specific inputs to an intermediate capability representation, a Template cache that functions as a standardized interface for capability injection, and a Template pipeline that loads, merges, and injects one or more Template caches into the base diffusion runtime. Because the interface is defined at the systems level rather than tied to a specific control architecture, heterogeneous capability carriers such as KV-Cache and LoRA can be supported under the same abstraction. Based on this design, we build a diverse model zoo spanning structural control, brightness adjustment, color adjustment, image editing, super-resolution, sharpness enhancement, aesthetic alignment, content reference, local inpainting, and age control. These case studies show that Diffusion Templates can unify a broad range of controllable generation tasks while preserving modularity, composability, and practical extensibility across rapidly evolving diffusion backbones. All resources will be open sourced, including code, models, and datasets.

### [86] [GradMAP: Gradient-Based Multi-Agent Proximal Learning for Grid-Edge Flexibility](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24549v1)
*Yihong Zhou,Hongtai Zeng,Thomas Morstyn*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多agent梯度近端学习，分布式训练通用方法可迁移

TL;DR: GradMAP通过嵌入可微三相AC潮流模型的梯度学习，实现了大规模电网边缘设备的完全分布式高效协调，训练速度比基线快3-5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 协调大规模电网边缘设备需要完全分布式的学习方法，同时尊重三相AC配电网的物理约束，现有方法在分布式和物理一致性方面存在不足。

Method: 提出GradMAP，为每个智能体独立训练神经网络策略，在训练中嵌入可微三相AC潮流模型，通过隐式微分传播约束违反，并使用动作空间中的近端替代加速梯度计算。

Result: 在IEEE 123总线馈线上1000个智能体案例中，GradMAP在15分钟内训练出分布式策略，实现最低约束违反，训练速度比基线快3-5倍，且样本外测试中运行成本和约束违反均最低。

Conclusion: GradMAP在训练效率和最终性能上显著优于现有基线，成功实现了大规模电网边缘设备的分布式物理感知学习。

中文摘要：协调大规模电网边缘设备需要学习方法在部署时保持完全分布式，同时尊重三相交流配电网的物理规律。本文提出基于梯度的多智能体近端学习（GradMAP）来应对这一挑战。GradMAP为每个智能体训练独立的神经网络策略，不进行任何参数共享，每个智能体仅使用自身局部观测进行在线决策，无需通信。在离线训练期间，GradMAP将可微的三相交流潮流模型嵌入到原始-对偶学习循环中，并利用隐式微分传播精确的网络约束违反，以更新策略参数。为了加速训练，GradMAP通过近端替代在更直接的策略输出（动作）空间中定义信任域，从而复用昂贵的环境梯度，这与PPO等其他工作中使用的概率分布空间不同。在包含1000个智能体（管理电池、热泵和可控发电机）的IEEE 123总线馈线案例研究中，GradMAP在单个工作站级NVIDIA RTX PRO 5000 Blackwell 48GB GPU上，15分钟内学习到最小化三相交流潮流约束违反的分布式策略。这比基于梯度的自监督学习基线实现了3-5倍的训练加速，并且训练效率显著优于多智能体强化学习基线。在样本外测试中，GradMAP也实现了最低的运行成本和约束违反。

Original abstract: Coordinating large populations of grid-edge devices requires learning methods that remain fully decentralised in deployment while still respecting three-phase AC distribution-network physics. This paper proposes gradient-based multi-agent proximal learning (GradMAP) to address this challenge. GradMAP trains independent neural-network policies for each agent without any parameter sharing, and each agent uses only its own local observation for online decision-making without communication. During offline training, GradMAP embeds a differentiable three-phase AC power-flow model in a primal-dual learning loop and uses implicit differentiation to propagate exact network-constraint violations to update the policy parameters. To speed up training, GradMAP reuses expensive environment gradients through a proximal surrogate within a trust region defined in the more direct policy-output (action) space, instead of the probability distribution space used in other works, such as PPO. In case studies with 1,000 agents managing batteries, heat pumps, and controllable generators on the IEEE 123-bus feeder, GradMAP learns decentralised policies that minimise three-phase AC load-flow constraint violations within 15 minutes of training on a single workstation-class NVIDIA RTX PRO 5000 Blackwell 48GB GPU. This is a 3--5x training speed-up over gradient-based self-supervised learning benchmarks and substantially better training efficiency than multi-agent reinforcement-learning benchmarks. In out-of-sample tests, GradMAP also delivers among the lowest operating cost and constraint violations.

### [87] [Cortex-Inspired Continual Learning: Unsupervised Instantiation and Recovery of Functional Task Networks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24637v2)
*Kevin McKee,Thomas Hazy,Yicong Zheng,Zacharie Bugaud,Thomas Miconi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出功能任务网络（FTN），通过自组织二元掩码和三级掩码生成过程实现块顺序持续学习中的参数隔离，在多个基准上几乎零遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 块顺序持续学习要求模型在无任务标签的情况下同时防止灾难性遗忘并高效推断当前输入对应的先前解决方案。

Method: 受新皮层启发的参数隔离方法，使用自组织二元掩码覆盖多个小深度网络。掩码通过梯度下降、平滑核和k-winner-take-all三步生成，确保不相交的梯度更新。

Result: 在三个持续学习基准上，FTN-Slow（细粒度平滑）几乎零遗忘；FTN-Fast（大核、少迭代）在速度与保留之间权衡。空间组织机制将掩码搜索复杂度从组合优化降低到近线性扫描。

Conclusion: FTN通过结构化的掩码生成和空间组织有效解决了块顺序持续学习中的遗忘和任务推断问题，实现了高效且近乎无遗忘的持续学习。

中文摘要：块顺序持续学习要求单个模型既保护先前解决方案免受灾难性遗忘，又在推理时无需任务标签就能高效推断哪个先前解决方案与当前输入匹配。我们提出了功能任务网络（FTN），这是一种受哺乳动物新皮层结构和动态模式启发的参数隔离方法。类似于混合专家模型，该方法使用一个高维、自组织的二元掩码覆盖大量小而深的网络，灵感来自锥体神经元的树突模型。掩码通过三个阶段生成：(1) 在连续掩码上进行梯度下降识别任务相关神经元，(2) 平滑核使结果偏向空间连续性，(3) k-winner-take-all 在固定容量预算下对得到的组进行二值化。与混合专家模型类似，每个神经元都是一个独立的深度网络，因此不相交的掩码恰好产生不相交的梯度更新，为抗灾难性遗忘提供了结构性保证。这个三阶段过程可以在单个梯度步骤中恢复先前训练任务的子网络，在推理时提供无监督的任务分割。我们在三个持续学习基准上进行了测试：(1) 合成的多任务分类/回归生成器，(2) 带有打乱类别标签的MNIST（纯概念漂移），(3) 置换MNIST（域漂移）。在所有三个基准上，使用细粒度平滑的FTN（FTN-Slow）几乎实现零遗忘。使用大核和仅2次平滑迭代的FTN（FTN-Fast）以牺牲部分保留为代价换取速度提升。我们展示了空间组织机制将有效掩码搜索从组合优化的top-k子集问题（复杂度O(C(H,K))）降低到对紧凑皮层邻域进行近线性扫描的复杂度（O(H)），并通过基于梯度的更新实现并行化。

Original abstract: Block-sequential continual learning demands that a single model both protect prior solutions from catastrophic forgetting and efficiently infer at inference time which prior solution matches the current input without task labels. We present Functional Task Networks (FTN), a parameter-isolation method inspired by structural and dynamical motifs found in the mammalian neocortex. Similar to mixture-of-experts, this method uses a high dimensional, self-organizing binary mask over a large population of small but deep networks, inspired by dendritic models of pyramidal neurons. The mask is produced by a three-stage procedure: (1) gradient descent on a continuous mask identifies task-relevant neurons, (2) a smoothing kernel biases the result toward spatial contiguity, (3) and k-winner-take-all binarizes the resulting group at a fixed capacity budget. Like mixture-of-experts, each neuron is an independent deep network, so disjoint masks give exactly disjoint gradient updates, providing structural guarantees against catastrophic forgetting. This three-stage procedure recovers the sub-network of a previously-trained task in a single gradient step, providing unsupervised task segmentation at inference time. We test it on three continual-learning benchmarks: (1) a synthetic multi-task classification/regression generator, (2) MNIST with shuffled class labels (pure concept shift), and (3) Permuted MNIST (domain shift). On all three, FTN with fine grained smoothing (FTN-Slow) results in nearly zero forgetting. FTN with a large kernel and only 2 iterations of smoothing (FTN-Fast) trades off some retention for increased speed. We show that the spatial organization mechanism reduces the effective mask search from the combinatorial top-k subset problem in O(C(H,K)) to the complexity of a near-linear scan in O(H) over compact cortical neighborhoods, which is parallelized by the gradient-based update.

</details>


### [88] [Learning to Think from Multiple Thinkers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24737v1)
*Nirmit Joshi,Roey Magen,Nathan Srebro,Nikolaos Tsilivis,Gal Vardi*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多源CoT监督学习及主动学习算法，与多agent协作学习场景相关，可迁移至coding agent训练。

TL;DR: 多个不同思考者的CoT监督在被动设置下难学，但主动学习算法可高效利用少量CoT数据学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多个思考者提供不同CoT时学习困难的原因，并探索如何高效利用多源CoT监督。

Method: 基于密码学假设证明被动设置下的难学性，并设计了一种主动学习算法，结合少量CoT数据和足量被动最终结果数据。

Result: 被动设置下，两个或少数不同思考者的CoT监督学习困难；主动算法中，每个思考者所需CoT数据量独立于ε，思考者数量为log(1/ε) log log(1/ε)，被动最终结果数据量为(1/ε)·poly log(1/ε)。

Conclusion: 多源CoT监督在被动学习中存在计算困难，但主动学习可有效克服，所需CoT数据量极小，表明主动交互对于利用多源推理链至关重要。

中文摘要：我们研究了多个思考者使用链式思维（CoT）监督的学习，所有思考者都提供正确但可能系统性地不同的解决方案，例如由不同思考者编写的数学问题的逐步解决方案，或解决同一问题的不同程序的逐步执行轨迹。我们考虑那些使用单一思考者的CoT监督在计算上易于学习，但仅使用最终结果监督（即没有CoT）难以学习的类别（Joshi et al. 2025）。我们证明，在密码学假设下，在被动数据收集设置中，使用两个或几个不同思考者的CoT监督学习可能是困难的。另一方面，我们提供了一种通用的计算高效主动学习算法，该算法使用每个思考者少量CoT数据（完全独立于目标精度ε）、中等数量的思考者（规模为log(1/ε) log log(1/ε)）以及足够多的被动最终结果数据（规模为(1/ε) · poly log(1/ε)）进行学习。

Original abstract: We study learning with Chain-of-Thought (CoT) supervision from multiple thinkers, all of whom provide correct but possibly systematically different solutions, e.g., step-by-step solutions to math problems written by different thinkers, or step-by-step execution traces of different programs solving the same problem.
  We consider classes that are computationally easy to learn using CoT supervision from a single thinker, but hard to learn with only end-result supervision, i.e., without CoT (Joshi et al. 2025). We establish that, under cryptographic assumptions, learning can be hard from CoT supervision provided by two or a few different thinkers, in passive data-collection settings.
  On the other hand, we provide a generic computationally efficient active learning algorithm that learns with a small amount of CoT data per thinker that is completely independent of the target accuracy $\varepsilon$, a moderate number of thinkers that scales as $\log \frac{1}{\varepsilon}\log \log \frac{1}{\varepsilon}$, and sufficient passive end-result data that scales as $\frac{1}{\varepsilon}\cdot poly\log\frac{1}{\varepsilon}$.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于 Nemotron 3 Nano 30B-A3B 骨干网络，结合创新的多模态令牌减少技术，采用 BF16、FP8、FP4 等多种格式的模型检查点，并公开部分训练数据和代码。

Result: 在真实世界的文档理解、长音频-视频理解和智能体计算机使用方面取得了领先结果，相比同类模型具有更低的推理延迟和更高的吞吐量。

Conclusion: Nemotron 3 Nano Omni 提供了一个高效、高性能的多模态模型，通过开放部分资源促进了进一步的研究与发展。

中文摘要：我们介绍了 Nemotron 3 Nano Omni，这是 Nemotron 多模态系列中的最新模型，也是首个原生支持音频输入以及文本、图像和视频的模型。Nemotron 3 Nano Omni 在其前身 Nemotron Nano V2 VL 的基础上，通过架构、训练数据和方法的改进，在所有模态上实现了持续的准确率提升。特别是，Nemotron 3 在真实世界的文档理解、长音频-视频理解和智能体计算机使用方面取得了领先结果。基于高效的 Nemotron 3 Nano 30B-A3B 骨干网络，Nemotron 3 Nano Omni 进一步采用了创新的多模态令牌减少技术，从而比同类大小的模型具有更低的推理延迟和更高的吞吐量。我们正在发布 BF16、FP8 和 FP4 格式的模型检查点，以及部分训练数据和代码库，以促进进一步的研究和开发。

Original abstract: We introduce Nemotron 3 Nano Omni, the latest model in the Nemotron multimodal series and the first to natively support audio inputs alongside text, images, and video. Nemotron 3 Nano Omni delivers consistent accuracy improvements over its predecessor, Nemotron Nano V2 VL, across all modalities, enabled by advances in architecture, training data and recipes. In particular, Nemotron 3 delivers leading results in real-world document understanding, long audio-video comprehension, and agentic computer use. Built on the highly efficient Nemotron 3 Nano 30B-A3B backbone, Nemotron 3 Nano Omni further incorporates innovative multimodal token-reduction techniques to deliver substantially lower inference latency and higher throughput than other models of similar size. We are releasing model checkpoints in BF16, FP8, and FP4 formats, along with portions of the training data and codebase to facilitate further research and development.

### [90] [Compute Aligned Training: Optimizing for Test Time Inference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24957v2)
*Adam Ousherovitch,Ambuj Tewari*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 测试时推理对齐训练方法，可应用于agent的测试时扩展策略。

TL;DR: 提出计算对齐训练，通过将训练目标与测试时推理策略对齐，显著提升LLM的测试时扩展性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准训练（SFT/RL）优化单个样本的似然，与测试时依赖聚合/过滤输出的策略不匹配，导致性能受限。

Method: 将推理策略视为基础策略上的算子，推导新的损失函数并实例化到SFT和RL中，实现训练与测试时策略的对齐。

Result: 实验证明该方法相比标准训练显著改善测试时扩展性能。

Conclusion: 计算对齐训练有效解决了训练与测试时策略的不匹配问题，提升了LLM在测试时计算下的表现。

中文摘要：扩展测试时计算已经成为增强大型语言模型（LLM）性能的强大机制。然而，标准的训练后范式，即监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL），在基础策略下优化单个样本的似然，这与依赖聚合或过滤输出的测试时过程产生了不一致。在这项工作中，我们提出了计算对齐训练（Compute Aligned Training），它将训练目标与测试时策略对齐。通过将推理策略概念化为基础策略上的算子，我们推导出新的损失函数，当应用这些策略时，能够最大化性能。我们针对常见的测试时策略，在SFT和RL中实例化了这样的损失函数。最后，我们提供了实验证据，表明这种训练方法相比标准训练显著改善了测试时扩展性能。

Original abstract: Scaling test-time compute has emerged as a powerful mechanism for enhancing Large Language Model (LLM) performance. However, standard post-training paradigms, Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL), optimize the likelihood of individual samples under a base policy, creating a misalignment with test time procedures that rely on aggregated or filtered outputs. In this work, we propose Compute Aligned Training, which aligns training objectives with test-time strategies. By conceptualizing inference strategies as operators on the base policy, we derive new loss functions that maximize performance when said strategies are applied. We instantiate such loss functions for SFT and RL across common test time strategies. Finally, we provide empirical evidence that this training method substantially improves test time scaling over standard training.

</details>
